### [92] [Euclean: Automated Geometry Problem Formalization with Unified Verification in Lean](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19374)
*Linbin Tang,Jingyan You,Zilin Kang,Hanzhang Liu,Sophia Zhang,Zenan Li,Chenrui Cao,Liangcheng Song,Jiaao Wu,Xian Zhang,Fan Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Euclean是一个四阶段框架，用于在原生Mathlib中自动形式化几何问题，构建了最大规模的Lean几何形式化数据集（OMNI-Geometry 768道竞赛题，Numina-Geometry 177,597题），验证了48.89% TOP1和73.33% TOP5的人类评估准确率，并将Goedel v2的证明成功率从13.6%提升至15.1%。代码和数据集已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有形式化推理系统在代数和数论（Lean）与几何（领域特定语言，形式化保障有限）之间存在严重割裂，增大了可信计算基并阻碍统一模型开发。已有的Lean几何形式化工作（LeanEuclid, LeanGeo）使用与标准Mathlib不兼容的公理系统，且规模极小（<1,100道题），无法支撑大规模训练。而直接在Mathlib中自动形式化几何面临独特挑战：隐式的图形假设（拓扑配置、非退化条件）必须显式化，且模型需适应Mathlib小型且快速演变的几何基础设施。

Method: 提出Euclean，一个四阶段框架：（1）约束显式化（constraint explication）——将隐式图形假设转化为显式约束；（2）配置锚定（configuration anchoring）——将几何配置锚定到Mathlib的现有结构；（3）形式化映射（formalization mapping）——将问题翻译为Mathlib兼容的Lean代码；（4）迭代修复（iterative repair）——自动检测并修复形式化错误。

Result: 构建了OMNI-Geometry（768道竞赛题）和Numina-Geometry（177,597道题），这是最大规模的Lean几何形式化数据集。人类评估显示TOP1准确率48.89%，TOP5准确率73.33%。基于该形式化数据训练Goedel v2，证明成功率从13.6%提升至15.1%。

Conclusion: Euclean成功实现了几何问题到原生Mathlib的大规模自动形式化，弥合了代数/数论与几何之间的形式化鸿沟。数据集质量和有效性通过人类评估和下流定理证明任务得到验证，为统一神经定理证明器的发展奠定了基础。

Abstract: Recent formal reasoning systems have reached IMO-level performance, yet they leave a fragmented landscape: algebra and number theory are handled in Lean, while geometry still relies on domain-specific languages with limited formal guarantees. This split increases the trusted computing base and hinders unified model development. Existing geometry-in-Lean efforts (LeanEuclid, LeanGeo) introduce custom axiom systems incompatible with standard Mathlib, and their small scale ($<$ 1,100 problems) limits large-scale training. Native Mathlib autoformalization of geometry, however, poses distinct challenges: implicit diagrammatic assumptions (e.g., topological configuration and non-degeneracy) must be made explicit rather than deferred to external solvers, and models must adapt to Mathlib's small, rapidly evolving geometry infrastructure. We present Euclean, a four-stage framework - constraint explication, configuration anchoring, formalization mapping, and iterative repair - for automatically formalizing geometry in native Mathlib. We construct OMNI-Geometry (768 competition problems) and Numina-Geometry (177,597 problems), the largest geometry formalization dataset in Lean. Human evaluation shows 48.89% TOP1 and 73.33% TOP5 accuracy. Training Goedel v2 on our formalizations improves proof success from 13.6% to 15.1%, validating dataset quality for unified neural theorem proving. Code and datasets: https://github.com/tlb-22/Euclean.

We also evaluate structural only learned models and a sanitized hybrid detector. The evaluation uses held-out provenance splits and paired benign-confounder controls. Structural-only learned mod els are weak under paired controls. A text-only TF-IDF model reaches perfect held-out scores but fails shortcut audits. ### [94] [HyGRL: Adaptive Hybrid Graph Reasoning for Multi-Entity Questions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19398)

TL;DR: 本文提出HyGRL框架，通过将非结构化文本嵌入结构化知识图谱构建异构网络，并采用模仿学习+强化学习的两阶段训练策略，在保持极低token成本和近实时推理的同时，在多实体组合问答任务上超越现有方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Multi-entity compositional questions pose significant challenges to existing retrieval-augmented language models. Conventional methods fall into a dilemma: standard RAG lacks dynamic reasoning, traditional Graph-RAG is limited by structural sparsity, and LLM-constructed Graph-RAG incurs prohibitive costs. We propose \textbf{\fwa}, a unified framework that embeds unstructured text into structured knowledge graphs, creating a heterogeneous network for flexible evidence retrieval. Reasoning is formulated as adaptive structure induction, learned via a robust two-stage process: (1) imitation learning distills heuristic expert signals, and (2) reinforcement learning refines the policy using LLM-driven preference rewards. Experiments demonstrate that {\fwa} effectively merges textual richness with structural knowledge, outperforming SOTA baselines in answer accuracy and reasoning fidelity while maintaining extremely low token costs and near real-time inference((code available at https://github.com/wjywjy123/HyGRL) .

</details>


### [95] [ITPEval: Benchmarking Formal Translation Across Interactive Theorem Provers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19407)
*Jiayi Wu,Robert Joseph George,Anima Anandkumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ITPEval，首个跨四大交互式定理证明器（Lean 4、Rocq、Isabelle、HOL Light）的自动形式化证明翻译基准，包含1,560个源文件与6,848个定理，并配套统一验证基础设施。评估结果显示，语句翻译最高pass@1为29.1%，证明翻译最高为10.5%；库不匹配是主要瓶颈；原生类型检查会高估语义保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式化定理证明中，不同系统间证明被隔离，缺乏跨系统翻译的评估基准，限制了基于学习的证明器的训练数据与验证结果的便携性。

Method: 构建ITPEval基准，包含受控层（公理化文件隔离翻译难度）与生态层（真实库暴露API与证明风格差异）；开发itpeval统一验证基础设施，支持状态隔离的预热后端；使用5种LLM在12个有向翻译对上评估语句与证明翻译；引入确定性Lean 4 BEq检查验证语义等价性。

Result: 语句翻译pass@1最高29.1%，证明翻译最高10.5%；受控定理证明pass@1为29.7%，生态层仅5.2%；54.0%的源头到Lean 4 miniF2F语句翻译通过BEq等价检查；Rocq和HOL Light比Lean 4和Isabelle更易作为形式化目标；多ITP上下文将Lean 4成功率从4.8%提升至10.6%。

Conclusion: 跨ITP证明翻译仍具挑战，库不匹配是主要瓶颈；原生类型检查会高估语义保真度；多ITP上下文有助于提升翻译效果；基准、基础设施与评估流程已开源。

Abstract: Formal theorem proving has emerged as a frontier challenge for machine learning, yet the ecosystem is fragmented: proofs remain siloed across incompatible systems, limiting both training data for learning-based provers and the portability of verified results. We present ITPEval, the first benchmark for evaluating automated formal proof translation across four major ITPs (Lean 4, Rocq, Isabelle, and HOL Light), spanning two distinct logical foundations. Our benchmark comprises 1,560 source files and 6,848 theorems organized into a controlled tier of axiomatized files that isolates foundational translation difficulty, and an ecosystem tier drawn from real libraries that exposes API and proof-style mismatches. We release itpeval, a unified multi-ITP verification infrastructure with state-isolated warm backends that preserve per-artifact native checking semantics. We evaluate both statement and proof translation across five frontier and open-weight LLMs on 12 directed translation pairs: statement translation peaks at 29.1% pass@1 and proof translation at 10.5%; controlled theorems reach 29.7% proof pass@1 versus 5.2% for ecosystem-level translations, confirming that library mismatch is the dominant bottleneck. In addition to pass@k evaluation, a deterministic Lean 4 BEq check establishes equivalence for 54.0% of verified source-to-Lean 4 miniF2F statement translations, showing that native type-checking alone can substantially overestimate semantic fidelity; in an autoformalization/auto-informalization round-trip study, Rocq and HOL Light are easier formalization targets than Lean 4 and Isabelle, while multi-ITP context improves pooled Lean 4 success from 4.8% to 10.6%. Our benchmark, verification infrastructure, and evaluation pipelines are publicly released.

*Om Narayan,Ramkinker Singh,Praveen Baskar*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了传统端点内容过滤器在有状态智能体架构下不足以防御持久化攻击；提出了包含诊断轨迹护栏、形式化时间验证、免疫记忆共识和硬件锚定信任的纵深防御分类体系。

Abstract: The transition from stateless generative models in artificial intelligence to stateful, autonomous agents represents an architectural evolution that, while providing the capabilities of long-term planning and the automation of enterprise workflows, also represents the introduction of a new form of security threat, the Chronos Vulnerability. The Chronos Vulnerability represents the threat of memory-based attacks, including the Memory Injection Attack (MINJA) and the sleeper agent, in which the internal belief system of the autonomous agent is compromised, effectively decoupling the attack vector from the final catastrophic event. This study formalizes the threat model for persistence-based attacks and the threat of Dynamics Blindness in the context of the World of Workflows benchmark, demonstrating that traditional endpoint content filters are insufficient for the current stateful architecture. Consequently, this study synthesizes a defense-in-depth landscape, categorizing emerging frameworks such as diagnostic trajectory guardrails (AgentDoG), formal temporal verification (Agent-C), immunological memory consensus (A-MemGuard), and hardware-anchored trust via GPU-based Trusted Execution Environments (TEEs) and Zero-Trust memory architectures.

### [98] [Sophisticated Policies from Epistemic Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19518)
*Wouter W. L. Nuijten,Bert de Vries*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文证明Sophisticated Inference的核心优势不在于树搜索本身，而在于其闭环结构——未来动作依赖于未来状态和观测。这种闭环形式可通过epistemic-prior变分自由能框架实现，并在Reactity Maze基准上验证：缺乏认知驱动或闭环结构的方法均无法成功，而同时具备两者的方法（包括Sophisticated Inference和全联合epistemic-prior主动推理）能解决环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清Sophisticated Inference（一种主动推理变体，常与递归信念建模和树搜索关联）的核心计算角色，论证其优势源于闭环控制结构而非树搜索本身，并展示该结构可在epistemic-prior变分自由能框架中表示。

Method: 将闭环结构分解为epistemic-prior变分自由能框架：认知先验提供主动推理目标，状态-动作联合后验提供状态依赖的控制结构。在Reactity Maze随机基准上比较三种变分目标（相同状态-动作后验族）、动作-状态因子化主动推理目标、Sophisticated Inference和标准EFE规划。

Result: 缺乏认知成分的方法不主动寻求信息；阻止未来动作依赖未来状态的方法无法将信息转化为可靠的目标达成。同时具备认知驱动和闭环推理的Sophisticated Inference和全联合epistemic-prior主动推理能解决环境任务。

Conclusion: Sophisticated Inference的优势并非树搜索所特有，而是源于主动推理的闭环形式。这种闭环形式可在epistemic-prior变分推理中表示，只需后验保持未来动作对未来状态的依赖性。

Abstract: Sophisticated Inference is a variant of active inference often associated with recursive belief modeling and tree search. We argue that its central computational role is simpler: within a planning horizon, it makes active inference closed-loop by allowing future actions to depend on future states and observations. This closed-loop structure can be represented in the epistemic-prior variational free energy framework. Epistemic priors supply the active-inference objective, while a joint posterior over future states and actions supplies the state-contingent control structure. We evaluate this decomposition in the Reactivity Maze, a stochastic benchmark designed to separate epistemic incentive from inner-horizon closed-loop control. The comparison includes three variational objectives with the same state-action posterior family, an action-state factorized active inference objective, Sophisticated Inference, and standard Expected Free Energy planning. The results show that neither ingredient is sufficient on its own. Methods without an epistemic component do not seek information, while methods that prevent future actions from depending on future states cannot turn information into reliable goal-reaching. By contrast, both Sophisticated Inference and full-joint epistemic-prior active inference solve the environment by combining epistemic drive with closed-loop inference. These results show that the advantage associated with Sophisticated Inference need not be specific to tree search itself. It arises from the closed-loop form of active inference, and this form can be represented in epistemic-prior variational inference when the posterior keeps future actions dependent on future states.

</details>


### [99] [Knowledge-Centric Self-Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19592)
*Xuefei Julie Wang,Lauren Hyoseo Yoon,Chengrui Qu,Amanda Zichang Wang,Atharva Sehgal,Eric Mazumdar,Yisong Yue*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种知识中心型自我改进（Knowledge-Centric Self-Improvement）范式，通过让通用可丢弃的智能体从任务中提取经验证据并蒸馏到持久化知识库中，实现跨任务、跨模型的性能提升，在推理、编程和终端基准测试中优于传统智能体中心型方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统智能体中心型自我改进将改进对象限定在智能体本身（如优化提示词、工作流或代码），导致改进成本高、维护困难且难以迁移。作者希望探索一种互补范式，将改进成果固化在持久化知识中，而非绑定到特定智能体设计或任务分布上。

Method: 设计简单协议：智能体先尝试执行任务，然后通过任务级论坛和跨任务论坛贡献基于证据的洞察，最后经过知识蒸馏将有效经验整合到共享知识库中。智能体保持通用且可丢弃，自我改进完全体现在知识库层面。

Result: 在抽象推理、编程和终端基准测试中，该协议相比智能体中心型基线提升了求解率并降低了成本；蒸馏得到的知识能够迁移到未见任务和不同LLM家族上，说明改进并非特定于LLM或运行实例。

Conclusion: 自我改进型智能体系统的进步可以主要由持久化知识驱动，而非依赖对智能体本身的持续优化；知识中心型方法具有更好的可检查性、可迁移性和可移植性。

Abstract: Self-improving AI systems typically treat the agent as the object that improves, by optimizing prompts, workflows, harnesses, or even the agent's own code. This agent-centric view can make improvements expensive to maintain and difficult to transfer, because gains become tied to a particular agent design, task distribution, or adaptation run. We study a complementary paradigm: knowledge-centric self-improvement, in which agents remain generic and disposable while the persistent object is a curated knowledge base that agents can leverage for future tasks. We conduct controlled case studies to operationalize this idea via a simple protocol. Agents attempt one task, then contribute evidence-grounded insights to a shared knowledge base via task-level and cross-task forums, followed by knowledge distillation. Because self-improvement is contained in the knowledge rather than the agent, improvement can be more inspectable, transferable, and portable. Across abstract reasoning, coding, and terminal benchmarks, this protocol improves solve rates while reducing dollar cost relative to agent-centric baselines. The resulting distilled knowledge also transfers to held-out tasks and across LLM families, indicating that the improvement is not merely an LLM- or run-specific behavior. These results support a new view of self-improving agentic systems: progress can be driven primarily by the curated persistent knowledge. Code is available at https://github.com/recursive-knowledge/KSI.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出六类静默失败分类法（模态捷径、幻影定位、错误证据正确答案、过度检索洗白、跨模态矛盾、来源幻觉），构建轨迹级诊断流程，在统一ReAct风格框架下评估答案正确性和证据依据质量。

Result: 在MMSearch-Plus轨迹上对四种前沿多模态模型的实验表明，表面准确率持续高估真实轨迹级正确性；通过交叉验证、空白图像压力测试和工具消融实验发现，静默失败与模型能力相关，且往往转移而非消失。

Conclusion: 多模态智能搜索系统的表面准确率不可靠，需要轨迹级诊断来揭示隐藏的失败模式；静默失败是能力依赖的，简单的修复可能只是将问题转移而非消除。

Abstract: Multimodal agentic search systems increasingly rely on external tools to answer knowledge-intensive visual questions. However, existing evaluations mainly focus on final-answer accuracy and may miss failures in the search trajectory. In this work, we study such hidden reliability issues as silent failures. We introduce a six-category taxonomy covering modality shortcuts, phantom grounding, wrong-evidence-right-answer cases, over-retrieval laundering, cross-modal contradiction, and provenance hallucination. Based on this taxonomy, we build a trajectory-level diagnostic pipeline that evaluates both answer correctness and evidence-grounding quality under a unified ReAct-style scaffold. Experiments on MMSearch-Plus trajectories across four frontier multimodal models show that surface accuracy consistently overestimates true trajectory-level correctness. We further use cross-judge validation, blank-image stress tests, and tool ablations to show that silent failures are capability-dependent and often shift rather than disappear. Home-page: https://github.com/DingWu1021/silent-failures-multimodal-agentic-search

### [103] [Rewarding Better Thinking for LLM Preference Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19824)

TL;DR: 本文提出Thinking Checklist Reward (TCR)，一种基于过程导向的奖励方法，通过将偏好对转化为样本特定的思考清单，并利用EMA残差公式分离出与结果奖励互补的思维盈余，从而改善强化学习中的偏好对齐，实验表明该方法在多个模型和基准上持续提升对齐性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将偏好对转化为样本特定的思考清单，用于评估生成推理轨迹是否满足偏好隐含的考量；引入指数移动平均(EMA)残差公式，分离出与结果奖励不可预测的互补思维盈余，减少与结果级监督的重叠。

Conclusion: TCR通过过程导向的思考清单奖励有效改善了偏好对齐中的轨迹级信用分配问题，为RL-based偏好对齐提供了更细粒度的过程监督信号。

Abstract: LLM preference alignment aims to optimize models toward human preferences across diverse user instructions. Reinforcement learning has become a major post-training approach for this goal, but existing proxy rewards are often outcome-level, mainly evaluating the final response while providing limited guidance for the reasoning trajectory. This can make credit assignment coarse when multiple responses receive similar final scores, leaving trajectory-level preferences under-specified. To address this limitation, we propose Thinking Checklist Reward (TCR), a process-oriented reward for RL-based preference alignment. TCR converts preference pairs into sample-specific thinking checklists and uses them to evaluate whether the generated reasoning trace addresses the preference-implied considerations. To reduce overlap with outcome-level supervision, TCR further introduces an exponential moving average (EMA) residual formulation to isolate a complementary thinking surplus beyond what is predictable from the outcome reward. Experiments on five models from three model families show that TCR consistently improves alignment performance across diverse benchmarks, with ablations further validating the importance of EMA-based residual formulation and sample-specific checklist supervision.

### [107] [Long-Term Sequential Decision Making under Risk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19914)
*Irmaan,Mirzanejad,Nadjet Bourdache,Abdel-Illah Mouaddib*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ERQDP方法，用于解决有限时域MDP在根式（坚定）风险目标下的规划问题。该方法无需枚举或采样，通过精确动态规划求解秩-分位数代理，在离散化回报网格上精确评估策略，并通过任意时间循环提供目标的上界-下界间隙（证书），在多个基准测试中返回带证书的解或显式残差间隙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ERQDP方法，包含三个核心部分：(1) 通过精确动态规划求解秩-分位数代理；(2) 在离散化回报网格上，通过精确DP计算回报概率质量函数（PMF）来评估候选策略；(3) 采用任意时间循环机制，逐步优化代理并报告目标函数的上界-下界间隙（证书），其中离散化预算的舍入误差有明确有界保证。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，ERQDP能够返回带证书的最优解或显式残差间隙；支持快速的风险参数扫描，大幅提升运行效率；同时兼容风险厌恶和风险寻求两种行为模式。

Conclusion: ERQDP是一种无需枚举和采样的高效方法，能够为有限时域MDP在根式风险目标下提供带证书的优化解，显著降低计算开销，并支持灵活的风险偏好设置。

Abstract: We study finite-horizon MDP planning under \emph{root-based} (resolute) risk objectives that apply a rank-dependent functional to the distribution of total returns. Such objectives are non-linear in the return distribution and generally break Bellman optimality, so direct optimization by scenario-tree enumeration is intractable. We propose \textbf{ERQDP}, an enumeration-free and sampling-free method that solves a rank--quantile surrogate via exact DP (Dynamic Programming), evaluates candidate policies exactly by DP over return Probability Mass Functions (PMFs) on a discretized return grid (with an explicit rounding bound), and refines the surrogate in an anytime loop that reports an explicit upper--lower gap (certificate) for the target objective up to discretization budgets. Across tested benchmarks, ERQDP returns certified solutions or explicit residual gaps, enables fast risk-parameter sweeps with substantial runtime gains, and supports both risk-averse and risk-seeking behaviors.

Abstract: Large metal-organic framework (MOF) databases support simulation, screening, and machine learning through crystallographic information files (CIFs). Both stem from weak coupling between chemical evidence and language-model explanation. Reward-guided reinforcement learning (RL) turns tool measurements into chemical explanation-level supervision, rewarding not only the final answer but also cited chemical evidence and evidence-supported diagnoses. We introduce Chemically Grounded Diagnosis (Chem-GD), a metric that assesses whether a correct diagnosis is explained by factual, relevant CIF-derived evidence. ### [109] [SenWorld: A Digital-Twin Simulation for Generating Context-Rich Evaluation Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19949)

Abstract: Smartphone personal assistants reason over longitudinal personal data, yet evaluating them requires context-rich evaluation data whose correct answers are known, and real device traces are too privacy-sensitive to share. To address this challenge, we present SenWorld, a physically grounded, deterministic, event-sourced digital-twin simulation that generates such data with ground truth fixed by construction. In SenWorld, personas live through a full day in a world built from real map, weather, holiday, and network data; every observable signal is archived in full-system snapshots; and each evaluation case is labeled by a pointer to an existing record rather than by post-hoc annotation or a large language model (LLM) judge. We evaluate this method with 16 personas in Beijing. The generated data closely matches the held-out real-user benchmark in category distribution (Jensen--Shannon divergence (JSD) 0.070) and in the daily rhythm of communication records (JSD below 0.1), though generated records remain shorter than real ones. Without scripted interaction, personas form a fully reciprocated dialogue subgraph and differentiated behavioral repertoires. Projected into 717 evaluation cases, the generated data exposes 78 failures in a production smartphone assistant, concentrating on call and Short Message Service (SMS) records while contacts, schedules, and alarms never fail. The snapshot pointer confirms each failure as an assistant-side retrieval error, with no LLM judge involved. Overall, SenWorld offers a privacy-safe, reproducible, and distribution-checked path to evaluation data whose labels are fixed by construction.

### [110] [EvoThink: Evolving Thinking in Large Reasoning Models via Self-Pruning and Aha-Moment Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19962)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LRM存在过度思考问题（冗余验证步骤），而现有缓解方法（如快慢思维切换、推理轨迹压缩）无法细粒度区分有益和冗余步骤，可能在追求效率时损害推理能力。本文旨在同时提升推理效率与能力。

Method: 提出EvoThink框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) 自剪枝训练（SPT），一种无监督方法，迭代剪枝冗余推理步骤并在精简轨迹上自训练；(2) Aha时刻偏好优化（AMPO），受遗传算法启发，识别有价值的失败推理尝试，合成从错误到正确的"aha时刻"数据，并优化模型内化该推理模式。

Result: 在数学推理和代码生成基准测试上的广泛评估表明，EvoThink不仅大幅减少了推理时的token消耗，还提升了LRM的推理能力。

Conclusion: EvoThink通过细粒度区分并消除冗余验证步骤，同时利用失败尝试中的有价值信息，实现了推理效率与能力的双重提升。

Abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) often suffer from overthinking due to redundant verification steps. Existing approaches for mitigating overthinking, such as fast-slow thinking switching and reasoning trajectory compression, fail to make a fine-grained distinction between beneficial and redundant steps within the LRM's reasoning process, and may thus impair reasoning capability in their pursuit of efficiency. To simultaneously improve reasoning efficiency and capability, we propose EvoThink, a framework that reduces redundant verification and encourages the exploration of new reasoning paths. EvoThink comprises two key components: Self-Pruning Training (SPT), an unsupervised method that iteratively prunes redundant reasoning steps and self-trains on the concise trajectories; and Aha-Moment Preference Optimization (AMPO), which, inspired by genetic algorithms, identifies valuable failed reasoning attempts, synthesizes from-wrong-to-right aha-moment data, and optimizes the model to internalize this reasoning pattern. Extensive evaluations across mathematical reasoning and code generation benchmarks demonstrate that EvoThink not only substantially reduces inference-time token usage but also improves the reasoning capability of LRMs.

</details>


### [111] [The Giant Hippocampus: From Structural Monoculture to a System of Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19973)
*Jaeho Seol*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出当前AI领域将所有任务统一使用Transformer架构的做法存在结构性错误，而神经科学证据表明不同认知功能依赖不同神经结构。作者提出应借鉴皮层异质性设计原则，构建由标准化接口连接的异构模块化网络（HetNet），将结构先验作为设计输入而非事后分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI领域将所有任务（文本、图像、语音）统一使用同一种架构（Transformer），与神经科学中皮层各区域具有不同细胞结构、执行不同功能的发现相矛盾。这种“结构误差”是可测量的，论文试图揭示其根源并提出替代方案。

Method: 论文通过跨学科分析（从Brodmann细胞构筑学到单细胞Patch-seq）建立结构-功能对应关系；追溯CNN的成功案例及其被抛弃的历史原因（Hardware Lottery）；对Transformer进行功能主义分析，论证其更类似海马体而非通用皮层；提出异构拓扑网络（HetNet）作为设计框架。

Result: 论证了：(1) 不同认知功能需要不同的结构先验；(2) Transformer本质上是海马体的功能模拟，不适合作为通用架构；(3) Mixture-of-Experts并未真正引入结构多样性；(4) 异构模块化网络（标准化接口连接、模块内保留特定归纳偏置）是更合理的设计范式。

Conclusion: AI架构设计应回归结构先验原则：在训练前明确指定模块化结构（而非统一模板），利用神经科学证据作为设计输入，构建“系统之系统”（System of Systems）——不同模块保留各自计算所需的归纳偏置，通过标准化接口通信。

Abstract: AI researchers describe state-of-the-art models as one thing repeated at scale: the Transformer, wired identically for text, pixels, or speech. Neuroscientists describe the cortex as a mosaic - dense Layer 4 in visual cortex for spatial encoding, thick Layers 5/6 in motion cortex for temporal integration - different jobs solved by different structures. This paper argues the gap is a structural error, not a stylistic one, and is measurable. A century of cytoarchitecture, from Brodmann to single-cell Patch-seq, shows distinct cognitive functions are implemented by qualitatively different structures, not by rescaling one template. The convolutional neural network is the field's own proof: local receptive fields and hierarchical depth encoded this prior directly, reaching strong image recognition on far less data than later architectures needed. The paper traces how this lesson was discarded: the "Hardware Lottery" made the Transformer the path of least resistance, not the principled choice, and Mixture-of-Experts, often cited as diversity, in fact partitions parameters among identical experts. A functionalist analysis shows the Transformer is best understood as a functional analog of the hippocampal formation, not a general-purpose cortex - the same mistake as treating cortex as one giant Broca's area, except the field has now standardized on a giant hippocampus, applied to tasks it was never built for: audition, executive gating, working memory. The paper closes with an alternative: a Heterogeneous Topological Network, a System of Systems in which distinct modules keep the inductive bias their computation demands and communicate through standardized interfaces. This is a design discipline for AI architects, not cognitive science: specify modularity before training, using structural evidence as a design input rather than reverse-engineering architecture from a trained model's behavior.

</details>

When a new disturbance occurs, a graph neural network-based retrieval mechanism identifies structurally similar past episodes, enabling experience-guided policy adaptation rather than learning from scratch. Experiments on dynamic flexible job-shop scheduling benchmarks with three disturbance types show that GSEM reduces makespan by 4.1%-10.0% and adaptation time by 33%-38% compared to the strongest memory-augmented baseline, with the advantage increasing under higher disturbance frequency. Abstract: Machine Learning models are widely used for automating classification tasks by extracting statistical patterns from data. However, their performance deteriorates if the data distribution changes, making them ill-suited to handle uncertain and evolving information. Moreover, they provide limited support for integrating prior knowledge. To address these limitations, we present CLARK (Closed-loop Learning for Adaptive Reasoning over Knowledge Graphs), a framework that integrates knowledge graphs, symbolic rule mining, and probabilistic reasoning under the Logic Programs with Markov Logic Networks (LP$^{\text{MLN}}$) formalism. Starting from CACTUS-derived KGs, CLARK translates graph structure into an LP$^{\text{MLN}}$ program and iteratively enriches it with candidate rules proposed by symbolic learners. We evaluate CLARK on two medical datasets, analysing both rule quality and downstream classification performance. Results demonstrate that CLARK leads to improved classification performance and more generalisable inference. Overall, CLARK provides a principled approach to constructing adaptive, interpretable, knowledge-driven models for classification.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (i) 将安全修复形式化为风险约束的干预决策问题，建模为CMDP，在最大化修复成功率的同时约束错误修复率(FRR)；(ii) 提出三维风险分解（爆炸半径、可逆性、认知不确定性），提供可解释的每动作安全接口；(iii) 设计上下文自适应的人机协作门控机制，将升级从二元保险转变为带宽感知的控制层，响应值班负载和业务关键性。策略从历史事件日志离线学习。

Conclusion: 通过将安全约束作为核心设计目标而非事后补充，所提框架在自动化修复的安全性与有效性之间取得了更优的权衡，有效减少了不必要的干预和人工升级负担。

Abstract: In modern IT operations (IT-Ops), the cost of an incorrect repair often exceeds the cost of no action at all. Yet existing automated remediation systems are designed to generate actions rather than to decide whether intervention is warranted, leaving safety as an afterthought enforced by manual approval. This paper makes three contributions to close this gap: (i) we reformulate safe remediation as a risk-constrained intervention decision problem and cast it as a Constrained Markov Decision Process (CMDP), in which the agent maximizes repair success subject to a bounded false remediation rate (FRR); (ii) we introduce a three-dimensional risk decomposition comprising blast radius, reversibility, and epistemic uncertainty, providing operators with an interpretable per-action safety interface; and (iii) we design a context-adaptive human-in-the-loop (HITL) gate that turns escalation from a binary failsafe into a bandwidth-aware control layer responsive to on-call load and business criticality. The full policy is learned offline from historical incident logs, enabling explicit control of the expected FRR. Experiments on the Train Ticket microservice benchmark with Chaos Mesh fault injection and an RCAEval-aligned fault taxonomy show that our framework reduces FRR by 39% while improving repair success by 2.5 points over a strong runbook baseline, and reduces on-call escalation load by 17% relative to a fixed-threshold variant.

Abstract: Design rule check (DRC) closure remains a major bottleneck in advanced-node physical design. Although detailed routers are rule-aware, residual design rule violations (DRVs) often require manual engineering change order iterations. Automating this process is challenging because repairs must account for complex geometric interactions, preserve circuit connectivity, and avoid introducing new violations. We present EvoDRC, a skill-evolution framework for agentic block-level DRC repair. EvoDRC decomposes the layout into bounded repair regions and assigns an LLM repair agent to each region. Local DRC analysis, connectivity-checking, and impact-preview tools provide feedback on proposed modifications. Repair operations and their resulting DRV changes are stored in a knowledge database and used to evolve the repair skills. Experiments on seven block-level designs from the DAC26 DRC Benchmark show that EvoDRC achieves a 73.5\% overall reduction compared to the reported baseline.

Abstract: Difference constraints of the form $x - y \leq d$ are well studied, with efficient algorithms for satisfaction and implication, because of their connection to shortest paths. Finite domain propagation algorithms, however, typically do not make use of these algorithms, and treat each difference constraint as a separate propagator. Propagation does guarantee completeness of solving, but can be needlessly slow. In this paper we describe how to build a (bounds consistent) global propagator for difference constraints that treats them all simultaneously. SAT modulo theory solvers have included theory solvers for difference constraints for some time. While a theory solver for difference constraints gives the basis of a global difference constraint propagator, we show how the requirements on the propagator are quite different. Crucially, we show how to explain propagations by a global difference constraint propagator, in order to use it within a lazy clause generation solver. We give experiments showing that treating difference constraints globally can substantially improve on the standard propagation approach.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large language models can answer scientific questions, yet a correct output does not reveal whether the model represents or uses the governing physics. Here we show that materials science mechanism information in the open-weight google/gemma-4-E4B-it model has three experimentally separable forms: concepts are readable in individual hidden states, constitutive orientation is carried by controlled transformations between states, and selected internal representations causally control engineering answers. We combine matched direct and Jacobian vocabulary readouts, option-free state geometry, a 60-law counterfactual benchmark and causal interventions. In 50 held-out materials descriptions, three independently fitted Jacobian lenses reproduced concept ranks, and target-free word sets from both readouts enabled blinded identification of 9 of 10 mechanism families. A separate 72-prompt benchmark produced mechanism-specific hidden-state neighborhoods, but an exact graph audit showed that this apparent physical organization was equally explained by numerical comparison. We therefore compared otherwise identical prompts in which only the direction of the physical input was reversed, asking whether the resulting hidden-state movement followed the supplied constitutive law. These state transformations ordered direct, physically neutral and inverse laws across 60 frozen relations and correctly oriented 39 of 40 directional laws, whereas lexical controls were near chance. Bidirectional interventions shifted answer probabilities toward or away from the physically appropriate outcome across all 12 matched cases, while counterfactual state patches transferred opposing decision signals across mechanisms and answer formats. Physical relationships were therefore more visible in controlled state changes than in absolute states alone.

Conclusion: PRO-LONG有效破解了长时域任务中信息保存与检索之间的权衡，以更高效的token使用实现了更优的性能。

Abstract: Long-horizon tasks require sustained perception, reasoning, and exploration, and are a persistent challenge for large language model (LLM) agents. This gap is reflected in their limited performance on continual learning benchmarks such as ARC-AGI-3, especially when models are evaluated out of the box. Various agent harnesses have been proposed to close this gap, and each commits to a strategy for handling long sequences of observations, i.e., what information to save from the environment and how to load it into model context, a choice we argue is particularly consequential. Existing methods for context management face a significant tradeoff, as preserving more information makes retrieving relevant details less tractable. We propose PRO-LONG, a minimal context management framework built around programmatic memory for LLM agents in long-horizon, exploratory settings. PRO-LONG addresses the tradeoff by keeping a complete, structured interaction log and capitalizing on recent progress in coding agents to search this history efficiently. On the full ARC-AGI-3 public game set, PRO-LONG improves over a base coding agent by an average of 18.0 percentage points across frontier models, and matches or exceeds state-of-the-art specialized harnesses (up to 76.1% pass@1) while using 4.2-5.8x fewer tokens. With Fable 5, PRO-LONG achieves 97.4% best@2 at a total cost of \$1,750. Relevant code and logs are available at https://github.com/alexisfox7/PRO-LONG.

</details>


### [119] [TRUST-ESD: A Risk-Calibrated and Governance-Aware AI Framework for Enterprise Strategic Decision Support Under Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20065)
*Tian Qiu,Li Yan,Mahabubur Rahman Miraj,Shanqin Yi,Md Intekhab Rahman Galib,Jahid Hasan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出TRUST-ESD，一个风险校准与治理感知的企业决策支持框架，通过反事实策略评估、共形不确定性校准、CVaR下行风险评分、风险记忆检索、策略即代码治理、可解释性和人工监督等模块，在不确定性下平衡价值、可靠性、风险暴露和合规性。实验表明，相比强基线方法，TRUST-ESD在风险调整效用、风险暴露、CVaR、校准误差、解释保真度和治理合规性等指标上均有显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业战略决策支持需要AI系统不仅准确，还需要具备不确定性感知、风险校准、可解释性和治理合规性，而现有预测导向方法仅通过最大期望效用选择行动，无法满足这些综合需求。

Method: TRUST-ESD框架包含以下核心模块：反事实策略的可预测效用估计、共形不确定性校准、基于CVaR的下行风险评分、风险记忆检索机制、策略即代码（policy-as-code）治理、可解释性分析以及人工监督。

Result: 相比强不确定性感知基线方法，TRUST-ESD在风险调整效用上提升7.95%，风险暴露降低23.22%，CVaR降低23.78%，校准误差降低13.89%，解释保真度提升10.90%，治理合规性提升9.76%，同时保持具有竞争力的预测精度。

Conclusion: 消融实验和案例研究进一步证实，不确定性校准、下行风险评分、风险记忆、可解释性和治理验证共同提升了可信赖的企业决策能力。

Abstract: Enterprise strategic decision support requires AI systems that are not only accurate, but also uncertainty-aware, risk-calibrated, explainable, and governance-compliant. This paper proposes TRUST-ESD, a risk-calibrated and governance-aware framework for enterprise decision support under uncertainty. TRUST-ESD evaluates feasible counterfactual strategies through predictive utility estimation, conformal uncertainty calibration, CVaR-based downside-risk scoring, risk-memory retrieval, policy-as-code governance, explainability, and human oversight. Unlike prediction-only methods that select actions by maximum expected utility, TRUST-ESD recommends strategies that balance value, reliability, risk exposure, and compliance. Experimental results show that TRUST-ESD improves risk-adjusted utility by 7.95%, reduces risk exposure by 23.22%, reduces CVaR by 23.78%, lowers calibration error by 13.89%, improves explanation fidelity by 10.90%, and increases governance compliance by 9.76% compared with strong uncertainty-aware baselines, while maintaining competitive predictive accuracy. Ablation and case-study analyses further confirm that uncertainty calibration, downside-risk scoring, risk memory, explainability, and governance validation jointly improve trustworthy enterprise decision-making.

</details>


### [120] [CUSUM-Shaped Inference-Time Monitoring and Targeted Re-Decoding for Quantized Small Language Model Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20129)
*El Hassane Ettifouri,Ayoub Belfatmi,Mahaman Sanoussi Yahaya Alassan,Walid Dahhane*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出MGT-B（监控引导的测试时回溯）方法，通过监控自回归推理模型的不确定性和退化特征，在检测到不良轨迹时回溯到合适位置并重新解码。在MATH-500数据集上的回顾性评估显示，240对时间顺序审计集准确率从82/240提升至88/240（+2.50个百分点，McNemar p=0.2632），467对历史覆盖集从146/467提升至167/467（+4.50个百分点，McNemar p=0.000753）。该方法在无警报时输出不变，有警报的轨迹中29次修正、8次回归。结果支持选择性监控-修复机制，但非确认性分析，也非理论保证的推理改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化小型自回归推理模型在推理过程中可能陷入长序列、重复或低效的轨迹，但现有的推理时计算分配方法通常不观察轨迹的实际发展情况。作者希望开发一种能够在推理过程中监控轨迹状态，并在检测到问题时进行回溯修复的机制，以提高推理质量。

Method: 基于早期token级别的e-CUSUM控制器，开发MGT-B（监控引导的测试时回溯）外部控制器。该方法将重叠窗口的预采样不确定性和退化特征映射到位置条件经验尾部概率，累积混合投注因子并使用CUSUM形状重置，当触发警报时估计回滚点，恢复token和KV缓存状态，执行约束重新解码。

Result: 在MATH-500数据集上，240对时间顺序审计集准确率从82/240提升至88/240（+2.50个百分点，McNemar p=0.2632，配对bootstrap 95%区间[-1.25, +6.25]）。467对历史覆盖集准确率从146/467提升至167/467（+4.50个百分点，McNemar p=0.000753）。316个无警报输出与原始版本完全相同，151个警报轨迹中包含29次修正和8次回归。

Conclusion: 该方法在MATH-500场景下支持选择性监控-修复机制的有效性，但并非确认性分析，经验因子未建立为有效的e过程或e检测器。该方法不是通用的或理论上可保证的推理改进方案。

Abstract: Quantized small autoregressive reasoning models can enter long, repetitive, or unproductive trajectories, yet inference-time compute is usually allocated without observing how a trajectory develops. Building on an earlier token-level e-CUSUM controller, we develop MGT-B (Monitoring-Guided Test-time Backtracking), a revised external controller that maps overlapping windows of pre-sampling uncertainty and degeneration features to position-conditional empirical tail probabilities, accumulates mixture betting factors with a CUSUM-shaped reset, and responds to an alarm by estimating a rollback point, restoring token and key-value-cache state, and performing constrained re-decoding. To audit whether the effect persists on problem identities first observed after the manual choice of log threshold h = 10, we retrospectively exclude 260 IDs present in pre-threshold artifacts and retain the chronologically first post-threshold pair for each remaining ID, yielding a 240-pair chronology-audit set. On this set, accuracy changes from 82/240 to 88/240 (+2.50 percentage points; 13 corrections, 7 regressions; exact McNemar p = 0.2632; paired bootstrap 95% interval [-1.25, +6.25]). A broader 467-pair historical-coverage set of seed-matched pairs changes accuracy from 146/467 to 167/467 (+4.50 points; McNemar p = 0.000753), but includes 200 seed-1 IDs available before or during threshold selection and is reported only as an exploratory estimate. All 316 no-alarm outputs in the 467-pair set are identical to vanilla, while the 151 alarmed trajectories contain 29 corrections and 8 regressions. Neither analysis is confirmatory, and the empirical factors are not established as a valid e-process or e-detector. The results support a selective monitoring-and-repair mechanism for the studied MATH-500 setting, rather than a general or theoretically certified reasoning improvement.

*Anmol Kankariya,Sercan Ö. Arık*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PoTRE是一个异构推理框架，通过四个推理代理（对抗精炼、分层规划、频谱搜索、直接链）的协同工作，配合任务自适应聚合层，在ARC-AGI-2、HLE和PRBench Finance三个基准上取得SOTA结果，在HLE上达到49.92%准确率，且推理效率优于同规模同质模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在需要长程规划和迭代纠错的复杂推理任务中表现不佳，且标准单流提示在面对新抽象概念或严格领域约束时脆弱易错。

Method: 将推理解耦为四个异构代理（对抗精炼、分层规划、频谱搜索、直接链），并通过任务自适应聚合层（候选选择、语义合成或神经符号验证）动态整合各视角产生全局鲁棒解。

Result: 在HLE上达到49.92%的SOTA准确率，超越此前最佳官方成绩；在ARC-AGI-2和PRBench Finance上表现优异；使用相似或更少推理token即可超越大规模同质基线模型。

Conclusion: 架构异构性能够以更高的推理效率（更少token）实现优于大规模同质模型的推理性能，验证了多视角推理协同的有效性。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) excel at many tasks, they frequently struggle with complex reasoning that requires long-horizon planning and iterative error correction. Furthermore, standard single-stream prompting proves brittle when models encounter novel abstractions or rigorous domain constraints. We introduce PoTRE (Poly-Topological Reasoning Ensembles), a heterogeneous framework that decouples inference into four agents: (1) Adversarial Refinement Agent, (2) Hierarchical strategic Planning Agent, (3) Spectrum Search Agent, and (4) Direct Chain Agent. A final Task-Adaptive Aggregation Layer dynamically reconciles these perspectives -- via final candidate selection, semantic synthesis, or neuro-symbolic verification -- to produce a robust global solution. We evaluate PoTRE on three frontier benchmarks: ARC-AGI-2, Humanity's Last Exam (HLE), and PRBench Finance. PoTRE achieves state-of-the-art accuracy of 49.92% on HLE, surpassing the previous best official score. We demonstrate that this architectural heterogeneity achieves improved reasoning performance using similar or fewer inference tokens compared to heavily scaled homogeneous baselines.

### [122] [Train the Model, Not the Reader: Decodability Supervision for Verifiable Activation Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20379)
*Hiskias Dingeto*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了自然语言自编码器对隐层激活的解释存在根本性缺陷：由于重构损失对具体虚假声明不敏感，高分解释可能只是捕获了“大意”而非真实事实。作者设计了RECAP方法，通过联合训练线性探针使指定内容保持可解码，从而大幅提升解释的可信度和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自然语言自编码器通过重构分数评估解释的忠实性，但该分数对单个虚假声明结构不敏感——翻转声明的后若重构不变则不受惩罚。需要验证该评估是否真正保证解释的逐条准确。

Method: (1) 分析了重构测试的局限性，证明在Qwen-2.5-7B上~98%的声明不依赖重构；(2) 在合成真实情况下发现标准方案5/5出现共适应私码；(3) 提出两种审计协议（grounded-vs-true cross和evaluator swap）；(4) 提出RECAP方法：联合训练线性探针与目标模型保持内容可解码；(5) 在Pythia-160M上验证跨模型泛化能力和对抗鲁棒性。

Result: Qwen-2.5-7B上~2%声明是重构依赖的，分数反映大意而非事实。RECAP使新verbalizer能真实陈述指定内容（代价+0.001 nat），在Pythia-160M上探针可解码但verbalizer仅部分传递（truth 0.44-0.46 vs 近零控制）。在对抗场景下，RECAP探针AUC 0.95（控制探针降至0.51）。

Conclusion: 高重构分数不能认证单个声明的忠实性；RECAP使指定内部内容可通过独立探针校验，为AI安全提供了一种防止模型通过编造解释来欺骗的方法。

Abstract: Natural-language autoencoders score explanations of hidden activations by reconstruction: an explanation is deemed faithful if the activation can be regenerated from it. The test is structurally insensitive to individual false claims: if flipping a claim does not change the reconstruction, the claim is never penalized. We show the test is passed in two ways, neither faithful. On a released Qwen-2.5-7B verbalizer, explanations reconstruct well above chance while ~2% of specific claims are reconstruction-dependent, so the score tracks gist, not specific facts. Under exact synthetic ground truth, the standard recipe develops co-adapted private codes (false wording the reconstruction depends on) in 5/5 runs, and fixes that leave the target model unchanged do not help. We contribute two audit protocols, the grounded-vs-true cross and the evaluator swap, and RECAP (Readable Encodings via Co-trained Auxiliary Predictors): linear heads trained alongside the target model to keep designated content decodable. On RECAP-trained sandbox models, fresh verbalizers state the designated content truly and the codes vanish, at a +0.001-nat cost. This replicates on a pretrained Pythia-160M: the content becomes reliably probe-decodable, though a fresh verbalizer conveys it only in part (truth 0.44-0.46 vs a near-zero control). For interpretability, high reconstruction does not certify individual claims. For AI safety, RECAP makes designated internal content independently checkable against probes rather than asserted by prose a model can game: an independent probe scores the verbalizer's true claims above its false ones (AUC 0.96, vs 0.82 without RECAP). Against an adversary that edits an explanation to maximize the reconstruction score while lying (suppressing ~87% of its lie penalty), the RECAP probe still flags the lies (AUC 0.95) while the control probe collapses to chance (0.51).

</details>


### [123] [SoftReason: A Fully Differentiable Neuro-Soft-Symbolic Deductive Reasoning Architecture over High-Dimensional Perceptual Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20402)
*Wael AbdAlmageed*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SoftReason提出了一种神经软符号架构，通过可微的演绎推理将感知（高维输入）与知识图谱提供的谓词逻辑无缝连接，核心创新是可微的即时推论算子，实现了从感知概率事实到逻辑闭包的端到端可训练推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经符号管道在感知和演绎之间存在离散接口导致的梯度断裂问题，使得神经网络无法端到端地学习推理过程。需要一种方法让推理过程完全可微，同时保留符号逻辑的结构化表达能力。

Method: 1) 将演绎状态表示为关于候选常量和谓词的局部软解释张量；2) 感知网络输出概率性基础事实，知识图谱三元组作为高置信度软证据输入；3) 核心创新：可微的即时推论算子——使用谓词定义嵌入和潜在组合通道形成软体谓词混合，聚合所有可能的见证，提出查询条件化的头部事实，通过单调概率OR更新解释。

Result: 在知识感知视觉问答（KVQA）任务上实例化，证明了SoftReason能够在单一可训练架构中支持端到端的感知基础、知识图谱证据注入和可微演绎闭包计算。

Conclusion: SoftReason成功弥合了感知与符号推理之间的梯度鸿沟，为需要同时利用感知数据和结构化知识的复杂推理任务提供了一个统一的、完全可微的解决方案。

Abstract: In many reasoning problems, the premises are not observed as discrete symbols, but must be inferred from high-dimensional inputs. Further, the predicate vocabulary, argument structure, and trusted evidence are supplied by a Knowledge Graph (KG), or rule definitions. Classical neuro-symbolic pipelines have a discrete interface between perception and deduction. We present a neuro-soft-symbolic architecture for differentiable deductive reasoning over latent perceptual facts and knowledge-provided predicates. SoftReason removes the gradient gap by representing the deductive state as a local soft interpretation tensor over candidate constants and predicates. Perception proposes probabilistic base facts, KG triples enter as high-confidence soft evidence, and every query anchor, predicate choice, and closure update remains differentiable. Our core innovation is a learned differentiable lift of the immediate-consequence operator. It uses predicate-definition embeddings and latent composition channels to form soft body-predicate mixtures, aggregate over all possible witnesses, propose query-conditioned head facts, and update the interpretation through a monotone probabilistic OR. We instantiate the framework on Knowledge-aware Visual Question Answering (KVQA), and demonstrates how SoftReason supports end-to-end perceptual grounding, KG evidence injection, and differentiable deductive closure in one trainable architecture.

</details>

### [125] [Emergent Autonomous Drifting for Collision Avoidance in Real-World Winter Driving Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19484)
*Elliot Weiss,Michael Thompson,Thomas Lew,John Subosits*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文研究了冬季真实驾驶条件下，漂移 maneuver 在安全性方面的最优性，提出了一个基于非线性模型预测控制（MPC）的漂移能力控制器，并在基于碰撞死亡数据的道路偏离和对向来车避撞场景中进行了仿真验证。与电子稳定控制（ESC）基准相比，漂移控制器能在稳定性和可控性之间权衡，更精确地应对危险冬季驾驶场景。蒙特卡洛研究表明，漂移控制器在多个速度下实现了更低的中位车道误差，且漂移主要出现在高速场景。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 漂移控制器能够在后轴遇到冰面时自然启动并维持漂移以保持在道路上，并能避开滑入本车道的对向来车；相比ESC，漂移控制器能牺牲稳定性换取可控性；蒙特卡洛研究显示漂移控制器在多个速度下中位车道误差更低，且漂移主要发生在较高速度下。

Conclusion: 具备漂移能力的控制器在冬季危险驾驶场景中具有显著的安全优势，尤其是在高速条件下，可以通过主动漂移 maneuver 更好地实现碰撞避让。

Abstract: Real-world collision avoidance is a core motivation for studying the dynamics and control of high sideslip drifting in vehicles, yet the practical benefit of such maneuvers has so far primarily been tested in scenarios explicitly engineered to require drifting. In this work, we explore the question of if and when drifting may be optimal for safety in real-world winter driving conditions. We present a drift-capable nonlinear model predictive control (MPC) system designed to handle scenarios grounded in crash fatality data and deploy the controller in a high fidelity simulator across road departure and oncoming vehicle collision avoidance scenarios. The controller naturally initiates and sustains drifting maneuvers to stay on the road when hitting a patch of ice on the rear axle and to avoid an oncoming vehicle that has slid into its lane. Comparisons with a benchmark electronic stability control (ESC) system demonstrate how a drift-capable controller can trade off stability for controllability to precisely maneuver through dangerous winter driving scenarios. A Monte Carlo study over random ice patches further shows that the drift-capable controller achieves lower median lane error than ESC across several speeds, while revealing that drifting emerges predominantly at higher speeds.

### [126] [Milo, a Fully Autonomous Indoor/Outdoor Robotic Guide Dog](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19530)
*Florian Golemo,Joanna Wolski,Joel Ruben Antony Moniz,Christopher Pal*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文介绍了Milo，首个开源、低成本（约2千美元）的机器人导盲犬平台，能够自主完成室内外导航、避障和避人，无需环境先验知识或外部计算，并与基线方法相比实现了更平滑的导航和更少的碰撞。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实导盲犬获取和维护成本高昂（约5万美元加持续开销）、等待名单长、寿命短，而现有的机器人导盲犬方案缺乏实际部署所需的自主性，依赖环境先验3D扫描、外部计算或对使用者感知有限。

Method: 基于改进的Unitree Go2机器人（搭载板载计算、传感器和手柄），结合体素地图、地面检测、障碍物检测和行人检测的感知栈，以及基于在自定义鸟瞰图模拟器中训练的避障策略的导航栈。

Result: 在真实室内外障碍物课程中评估，相比基于costmap的基线方法，Milo实现了更平滑的导航和更少的与使用者碰撞。

Conclusion: Milo作为首个开源低成本自主机器人导盲犬平台，展示了满足导盲犬核心协同导航角色的潜力，并通过完全开源硬件指令和软件栈以最大化对盲人和低视力人群的可及性。

Abstract: Many Blind and Low-Vision (BLV) people rely on guide dogs for moment-to-moment navigation, such as staying on path and avoiding obstacles and pedestrians. However, guide dogs are expensive to acquire and maintain (approximately \$50k USD plus ongoing costs), often involve long waiting lists, and have relatively short life expectancies. While robot guide dogs offer a promising alternative, existing approaches exploring this idea suffer from several drawbacks: They often lack the autonomy required for real-world deployment, relying on prior 3D scans of the environment, external computation, or limited awareness of the handler. In this work, we present Milo, the first open-source, low-cost (approximately \$2k USD) robotic guide dog platform capable of fulfilling the basic collaborative navigation role expected of a guide dog. Milo is fully autonomous, requiring no a priori knowledge of the environment, completely self-contained with all computation performed onboard, and suitable for both indoor and outdoor navigation while avoiding obstacles and pedestrians. Our system consists of a modified Unitree Go2 robot (equipped with onboard compute, sensors, and a handle), a perception stack combining voxel mapping with floor, obstacle, and pedestrian detection, and a navigation stack based on an obstacle-avoidance policy trained in a custom bird's-eye-view simulator. We evaluate Milo in real indoor and outdoor obstacle courses and compare it against a costmap-based baseline, demonstrating smoother navigation and fewer handler collisions. To maximize accessibility for BLV users, we release both the robot hardware instructions and the complete software stack as open source.

Motivation: 现有触觉引导系统采用预定义干预策略，无法适应不同用户和应用场景的多样化安全偏好，需要手动试错设计。

Result: 仿真和硬件实验表明，该框架能从稀疏用户输入中学习个性化安全干预，并减少生成触觉反馈与演示偏好之间的不匹配。

Existing haptic guidance systems typically employ predefined intervention strategies that cannot accommodate the diverse safety preferences of individual users or application scenarios. To address this limitation, we propose a Learning from Haptics (LfH) framework that learns user-preferred safety interventions from sparse demonstrations, eliminating the need for manual trial-and-error design. Our framework is built on a differentiable Control Barrier Function (CBF)-based optimization layer that automatically adjusts the underlying safety parameters to match the demonstrated haptic responses. Instead of tuning controller parameters directly, users teach the system how they expect it to intervene during teleoperation. The resulting haptic guidance reflects the demonstrated intervention preferences while preserving the intuitive interaction of haptic shared control. Simulation and hardware experiments demonstrate that the proposed framework can learn personalized safety interventions from sparse user input and reduce the mismatch between the generated haptic feedback and the demonstrated preferences.

### [128] [LENS: LLM-guided Environment Simplification for Planning and Control in Clutter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19633)
*Aileen Liao,Rachel Holladay,Dinesh Jayaraman,Michael Posa*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出LENS（LLM引导的环境简化方法），通过自动生成场景特定、任务特定且自适应更新的抽象表示，对杂乱环境中的机械臂操作进行去杂简化，从而提升经典规划、模型控制以及视觉-语言-动作模型在复杂多物体操作任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通用机器人操作方法在处理真实世界多物体杂乱场景时面临挑战：物体碰撞、不可预测接触物理、干扰物及任务歧义导致问题复杂度急剧上升。虽然场景抽象是弥合这一鸿沟的关键，但当前生成抽象表示需要大量任务特定的人工工程，成本高、难以调整且无法规模化。

Method: LENS是一种即插即用的方法，在现有规划和控制栈之上自动生成场景特定、任务特定且自适应更新的抽象表示。具体而言，LLM通过闭环方式根据任务进展对场景实体进行合并（如堆叠物体）或剪枝（如远处物体），从而产生去杂后的抽象场景表示。

Result: 实验表明，LENS能够提升经典规划、基于模型的控制以及视觉-语言-动作模型等一系列方法在多种高度杂乱操作场景中的表现。

Conclusion: LENS提供了一种高效、可扩展的场景抽象生成方案，有效缩小了机器人操作从实验室到真实部署的差距，验证了LLM引导的动态场景简化在杂乱环境中的通用性和有效性。

Abstract: Despite recent advances in general-purpose robotic manipulation, real-world multi-object clutter remains challenging to handle for today's prevalent approaches. The problem scales in complexity due to more objects and collisions, more unpredictable contact physics, distractors, and task ambiguity. Bridging this gap to real-world deployment requires effective scene abstractions; yet today, producing such abstractions requires extensive task-specific manual engineering, which does not scale. These abstractions are costly to generate and difficult to adjust or fine-tune. We instead propose a plug-and-play fix to automatically generate scene-specific, task-specific, adaptively updating abstractions on top of existing planning and control stacks. LLM-guided Environment Simplification (LENS) produces a de-cluttered abstracted scene representation by merging (e.g., stacked objects) or pruning (e.g., distant objects) scene entities in a closed loop in response to task progress. These dynamic, task-relevant abstractions are versatile and easy to use. In our experiments, we show that LENS improves classical planning, model-based control, and a vision-language-action model, across a diverse set of highly cluttered manipulation scenes. Project website: https://lens-2026.github.io/.

This enables real-time, decentralized collision avoidance while preserving mission objectives and scalability. Conclusion: 当前智能体远未解决跨场景导航问题，室内外环境适应仍面临重大挑战，需要进一步研究。

Existing benchmarks usually evaluate indoor and outdoor navigation separately, and many abstract away robot execution, leaving exit finding, boundary traversal, adaptation, and kinodynamic failures underexplored. We introduce NavVerse, a physics-enabled benchmark for indoor-to-outdoor embodied navigation. NavVerse contains 100 indoor scenes, 50 urban outdoor scenes, and 50 indoor-to-outdoor scenes, and 10,000 episodes spanning Object Navigation, Vision-and-Language Navigation, and Place Navigation tasks, where agents search for semantic points of interest such as restaurants or banks. ### [131] [Contact-Persistent Full Actuation for Aerial Physical Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19708)
*Abhimanyu Khadga,Abhinav Sinha,Shashi Ranjan Kumar*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出"接触持久全驱动"控制框架，证明多旋翼无人机在持续接触交互中，全驱动不仅取决于控制分配矩阵的秩条件，更取决于任务力矩在可行力矩多胞体中的内点性质，并引入残差权限半径作为量化指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于秩条件或自由飞行跟踪性能的全驱动认证方法，无法保证无人机在持续物理接触交互中的完全可控性，因为部分力矩被交互任务消耗，仅剩残余力矩可用于稳定、扰动抑制和机动。

Method: 将$\mathbb{R}^3 \times \mathrm{SO}(3)$上的刚体模型与依赖形态的力矩映射结合，统一描述固定倾角、变倾角、同轴和过驱动等多种多旋翼架构；定义可行力矩集、残余力矩集和残差权限半径；提出残差边界证书、松弛最大化分配证书和鲁棒可实现性条件。

Result: 接触持久全驱动等价于任务力矩位于约束可行力矩多胞体的内部，残差权限半径恰好为该点到多胞体边界的距离；数值实验表明，全行秩不足以保证可行接触操作，中等倾角可保持残差权限，过小或过大倾角因侧向力不足或悬停裕度损失而失效。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架为接触交互场景下的无人机驱动能力认证提供了比传统秩条件更严格的定量判据，并可作为安全滤波器的理论依据。

Abstract: Fully actuated unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) are usually certified through rank conditions on a control-allocation matrix or through free-flight tracking performance. For aerial physical interaction, this certification may be incomplete. During sustained contact, part of the available wrench is consumed by the interaction task, and only the residual wrench remains available for stabilization, disturbance rejection, and maneuvering. This paper introduces a control-theoretic framework for \emph{contact-persistent full actuation}. A rigid-body model on $\R^{3}\times\SO\left(3\right)$ is combined with a morphology-dependent wrench map that captures fixed-tilt, variable-tilt, coaxial, and overactuated multirotor architectures. We define feasible wrench sets under actuator limits, residual wrench sets under task loading, and residual authority margins that strengthen the usual rank-based notion of full actuation. The main result shows that contact-persistent full actuation is equivalent to interiority of the task wrench in the constrained feasible wrench polytope, and that the residual authority radius is exactly the distance to the polytope boundary. We further introduce a signed residual-margin certificate for infeasible and boundary cases, a slack-maximizing allocation certificate, and a robust implementability condition that can be used as a margin-aware safety filter. Numerical evaluation on an abstract tilted hexarotor shows that full row rank alone does not imply feasible contact operation. Intermediate tilt angles preserve residual authority during pushing, whereas small or excessive tilts fail because of lateral-force deficiency or hover-margin loss.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分布式缆索驱动产生行进波，可编程被动柔顺性实现鲁棒的接触丰富的运动；滚动关节使弯曲平面沿身体重新定向，实现快速重构和运动模式间平滑过渡，并配备齿轮锁定以在无持续动力下保持形态。

Recent designs incorporating compliance demonstrate robust locomotion without complex sensing or control; however, these systems typically rely on fixed body configurations, with each morphology specialized for a single locomotion mode or environment. This raises a key challenge: how can a single limbless robot achieve versatile locomotion while preserving the robustness of compliance-mediated locomotion? To address this challenge, we present a cable-driven limbless robot that reconfigures body morphology and compliance to enable diverse locomotion modes. Distributed cable actuation generates traveling body waves, while programmable passive compliance enables robust contact-rich locomotion without terrain knowledge or high-bandwidth feedback. Rolling joints reorient bending planes along the body, enabling rapid reconfiguration and smooth transitions between locomotion styles, and incorporate geared locking to maintain configuration without continuous power. By combining programmable bending compliance and morphology control, the platform achieves lateral undulation, sidewinding, rolling, and twisting within a single system. Experiments demonstrate reliable gait generation, traversal in obstacle-rich environments, and transitions between modes, establishing a versatile limbless platform for navigating complex environments with applications in search and rescue, environmental monitoring, and inspection.

### [133] [EgoRecovery: Acquiring Failure Recovery Ability Through Human Recovery Demonstration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19745)
*Zuhao Ge,Yuchen Zhou,Weitao Zhou,Minglei Li,Xinyu Li,Chao Wu,Hanwen Zhao,Haotian Wang,Zuxuan Wu,Xiaosong Jia,Yu-Gang Jiang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出利用人类示教数据（尤其是失败恢复过程）来训练机器人恢复策略，通过EgoRecovery框架将人类恢复演示与机器人数据对齐到共享的修正意图空间，从而仅需少量机器人恢复数据即可实现高效的失败恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人需要在非结构化和嘈杂的真实环境中从失败中恢复并重试任务，但通过遥操作收集恢复数据难以规模化，因为诱导失败状态、执行纠正动作和重置环境非常耗时，且失败模式多样，需要远多于成功演示的恢复数据。

Method: 利用第一人称人类数据捕捉失败恢复过程；提出EgoRecovery共训练框架，将人类恢复演示与机器人数据对齐到紧凑的修正意图空间（捕捉纠正的时机和幅度）；使用少量机器人恢复演示将意图映射为可执行的机器人动作；部署时通过学习恢复门（recovery gate）预测何时需要纠正并激活修正意图。

Result: 人类操作员在相同时间内可生成比机器人遥操作多10倍以上的有效恢复数据；在真实世界恢复任务中，EgoRecovery在从失败状态恢复的成功率上优于纯机器人恢复、直接人类-机器人数据共训练以及直接意图迁移基线。

Conclusion: 人类第一人称失败恢复数据是训练机器人恢复策略的可扩展替代方案，EgoRecovery框架能有效弥合人-机具身差异，实现高效的机器人失败恢复。

Abstract: Robust embodied robots should be able to recover from failures and retry tasks in order to operate reliably in unstructured and noisy real-world environments. Achieving this capability requires training policies on data that captures recovery behaviors. However, collecting such data through robot teleoperation is difficult to scale, as it is time-consuming to induce diverse failure states, perform corrective actions, and reset the environment. This challenge is further exacerbated by the high diversity of failure modes, which demands substantially more recovery data than success demonstrations. In this work, we show that egocentric human data capturing failure recovery processes provides a scalable alternative. By efficiently arranging task-level failure configurations and recording short recovery segments, human operators can generate more than 10x as much valid recovery data per hour compared to robot teleoperation under our protocol. To address the embodiment gap between human and robot, we propose EgoRecovery, a co-training framework for learning recovery behavior, where human recovery demonstrations are aligned to a compact corrective-intent space shared with robot data, which captures the timing and magnitude of correction. Only a small number of robot recovery demonstrations are required to connect this intent to executable robot actions. At deployment, a learned recovery gate predicts when correction is needed from robot observations and activates the corrective intent only in recovery states. Experiments on real-world recovery tasks show that EgoRecovery improves success from failure starts over robot-only recovery, direct co-training with human recovery data, and direct intent-transfer baselines.

### [134] [Defer to Plan: Adaptive Multi-Agent Fusion for End-to-End V2X Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19774)
*Nuoran Li,Zhang Zhang,Yueran Zhao,Tianze Wang,Chao Sun*

TL;DR: 提出了一种端到端协作驾驶系统V2X-AD，通过MotionNetwork融合时序信息、注意力机制压缩空间特征、自回归解码器融合多智能体特征以及MoE架构增强异构特征表示能力，在闭环评估中驾驶得分79.72，比SOTA基线CoDriving(77.15)提升3.33%，同时保持通信效率。

Motivation: 现有协同感知方法仅优化模块级感知能力，无法有效服务于最终的规划和控制任务，亟需一种直接优化规划任务性能的端到端协作驾驶系统。

Method: 1) MotionNetwork融合历史时序信息；2) 注意力机制将空间特征压缩为紧凑token；3) 自回归解码器自适应融合多智能体特征；4) Mixture-of-Experts (MoE)架构增强异构特征表示能力。

Result: 驾驶得分79.72，超越SOTA基线CoDriving(77.15) 3.33%，保持通信效率。

Conclusion: 端到端直接优化规划任务相比模块级感知优化能更有效提升自动驾驶性能，MoE架构和自回归融合机制对异构多智能体特征建模有效。

Abstract: Vehicle-to-everything-aided autonomous driving (V2X-AD) significantly enhances driving performance through information sharing. However, existing collaborative perception methods only optimize module-level perception capabilities and fail to effectively serve the ultimate planning and control tasks. We propose an end-to-end collaborative driving system that directly optimizes planning task performance. The system employs MotionNetwork to fuse historical temporal information, utilizes attention mechanisms to efficiently compress spatial features into compact tokens, and adaptively fuses multi-agent features through an autoregressive decoder. Additionally, we introduce Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architecture to enhance the model's representation capacity for heterogeneous features. Experiments demonstrate that our method achieves a driving score of 79.72, surpassing the state-of-the-art CoDriving baseline (77.15) by 3.33% in closed-loop evaluation while maintaining communication efficiency.

</details>


### [135] [V2F: Vision-Informed Grasp Force Prediction for Damage-Aware Robotic Handling of Date Fruits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19804)
*Shahd Shami,Obadah Wali,Eric Feron,Shinkyu Park*

Method: 首先对椰枣样本进行力学表征，建立安全抓取包络并量化果实几何与生物屈服应力的关系；然后构建V2F管线：计算机视觉分割→主动轮廓细化和几何特征提取→物理信息残差神经网络（增强Hertz接触方程），输入为视觉描述符和栽培品种元数据，输出安全抓取力。

Abstract: This paper presents a vision-informed grasp force prediction framework for robotic handling of date fruits. The resulting model maps non-contact visual descriptors and cultivar metadata to predict a safe grasp force with mean validation performance of $R^2 \approx 0.7$ across unseen cultivar groups, which is a good result given the inherent mechanical variability of biological tissue. Experimental validation using a gripper and load cell indicates that the predicted forces enable stable manipulation of different types of date fruits, with residual deformations below 1 mm and no observable damage. These results show that pre-emptive, vision-driven force estimation% can replace slow and potentially damaging tactile exploration , enabling safer robotic handling of fragile fruits.

SOPD introduces an entropy-based token selection mechanism that uses teacher uncertainty to identify socially informative decision tokens, while suppressing gradients from low-entropy tokens corresponding to trivial navigation states. A temperature-controlled Jensen-Shannon divergence objective is then used to align the student and teacher distributions on the selected tokens. These results suggest that SOPD is an effective strategy for building lightweight yet socially aware VLM-based navigation systems.

Method: 构建KineBench基准：级联视觉基础模型从生成视频帧中直接提取6D末端执行器位姿，在物理模拟器中执行；引入SPARC和Maruyama Manipulability Index两个3D运动学指标；基于ManiSkill3的20个操作任务构建四个渐进评估套件。

Abstract: Evaluating the physical consistency of embodied world models(EWMs) is a critical open challenge. Due to the intricate mapping from 2D pixel space to 3D kinematic space, the learned IDMs can be brittle to data outside their training distribution, resulting in unreliable action extraction from the generated videos with novel objects and scenarios. This creates an unavoidable attribution ambiguity between world model inaccuracies and extractor errors. To reduce this ambiguity, we present KineBench, an IDM-free closed-loop benchmark for EWMs, built upon an explicit kinematic grounding pipeline. Given a generated video, KineBench employs cascaded visual foundation models to directly extract 6D end-effector poses from individual frames, which are then executed in a physics simulator for closed-loop validation. Beyond execution-based task success, KineBench incorporates two classical 3D kinematic metrics--Spectral Arc Length (SPARC) and the Maruyama Manipulability Index--to characterize trajectory smoothness and kinematic feasibility from a robot-centric perspective. Built on 20 diverse manipulation tasks in ManiSkill3, KineBench evaluates EWMs across four progressive suites: basic execution, task transfer, visual out-of-distribution generalization, and complexity-conditioned scaling. Evaluation across frontier models reveals task-complexity-bounded nonlinear scaling in embodied video generation, providing empirical guidance for future data-scaling strategies.

### [141] [Diffusion ReRoll: Revisable Denoising for Robotic Sequential Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19919)
*Seonsoo Kim,Seongil Hong,Jun-Gill Kang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Diffusion ReRoll提出了一种可修正的扩散去噪框架，通过在保持部分区域继续去噪的同时选择性地重新加噪局部稳定区域，实现跨时间步的迭代修正，在长时程规划、策略学习和统一视频-动作建模任务上相比现有方法（如Diffusion Forcing、Diffuser、Diffusion Policy）取得了显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散的序列预测器通常执行单一单调的去噪过程，缺乏跨时间步的迭代修正能力，导致早期预测错误无法被后续信息修正。

Method: Diffusion ReRoll通过结构化重加噪机制，选择性地对已局部稳定的区域重新加噪，使其能够利用其余序列区域的上下文信息进行再次细化，实现早期段与后期段之间的相互修正，同时保持局部一致性。

Result: 在OGBench PointMaze和AntMaze上，相比Diffusion Forcing在引导规划中平均成功率提升21%，相比Diffuser在目标修复中提升23%。在LIBERO-10多任务基准上，比Diffusion Policy平均成功率提升56.5%。在统一视频-动作预测中，策略和逆动态性能提升，尤其在分布外评估下最优，并实现了最佳的动作-视频一致性。

Existing diffusion-based sequence predictors typically perform a single monotonic denoising process. In contrast, Diffusion ReRoll selectively re-noises regions that have become locally stable while the remaining regions continue denoising, so the re-noised regions can be refined again using context from the rest of the horizon. This structured re-noising enables iterative cross-horizon revision, allowing earlier and later segments to revise one another, while maintaining local consistency. We evaluate Diffusion ReRoll against full-sequence diffusion and causal denoising based on Diffusion Forcing across long-horizon planning, policy learning, and unified video-action modeling. On OGBench PointMaze and AntMaze, Diffusion ReRoll achieves relative gains in average success rate of 21% over Diffusion Forcing in matched guidance-based planning and 23% over Diffuser in matched goal-inpainting. In diffusion-policy-style action prediction, Diffusion ReRoll improves average success by 56.5% relative to Diffusion Policy across different prediction horizons and history lengths on the LIBERO-10 multi-task benchmark. In unified video-action prediction, Diffusion ReRoll improves policy and inverse dynamics performance, especially under out-of-distribution evaluation, and achieves the best action-video consistency. These results support structured re-noising as an effective mechanism for revisable robotic sequence generation.

### [142] [Unified Prediction and Planning via Conflict-Aware Disjoint Parameter Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19971)
*Taewon Seo,Seonae Jeon,Giwon Lee,Kuk-Jin Yoon,Daehee Park*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 针对社交机器人导航中运动预测与运动规划的任务冲突问题，提出基于模型合并的Disjoint Parameter Training（DPT）框架，通过分布式参数学习分离各任务的关键参数区域，并结合稀疏合并策略，在资源受限的边缘设备上实现紧凑统一模型的高效协同推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有紧凑型统一模型在共享编码器架构下，由于预测邻居行为与自我安全规划的目标不同，存在严重的表征冲突（Skill Conflict），即不同任务竞争相同权重导致模型无法充分专业化各自技能。

Method: 提出DPT框架：1）分布式参数学习——分离各任务的关键参数区域，保留核心能力后再合并；2）稀疏合并——仅选择性整合每个任务最具影响力的参数，而非合并所有任务参数，从而防止相邻特征干扰并集中表征能力。DPT可并行应用于多种合并方法。

Result: 在JRDB和JTA标准人群导航基准上，DPT框架展现出优越性能，验证了其通用性和有效性。

Conclusion: DPT有效解决了统一模型中运动预测与运动规划之间的S kill Conflict问题，为资源受限环境下安全、高效的机器人导航提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Accurate motion prediction of surrounding agents and safe motion planning are two closely coupled key tasks for social robot navigation in crowded environments. Deploying these systems on resource-constrained edge devices necessitates compact, unified models that can perform both tasks simultaneously. However, within these compact shared encoders, recent unified models often overlook severe representational conflicts that arise from the distinct objectives of predicting neighbor behaviors versus ego-centric safety planning. To address this issue, we first identify the Skill Conflict$\unicode{x2014}$a phenomenon where overlapping parameter assignments cause distinct tasks to compete for the same weights, preventing the model from fully specializing in individual skills. To resolve this, we propose a novel model-merging-based framework, Disjoint Parameter Training (DPT). DPT mitigates performance degradation caused by Skill Conflict through distributed parameter learning, which separates the key parameter regions of each task while preserving their core capabilities prior to merging. In addition, we observe that sparse merging, which selectively integrates only the most influential parameters for each task rather than combining all task-specific parameters, yields optimal performance by preventing interference among adjacent features and concentrating representational capacity. DPT can be applied in parallel with a variety of merging methods. Evaluated on standard crowd navigation benchmarks (JRDB and JTA), our framework demonstrates superior performance, validating its versatility and effectiveness for safe, resource-efficient robot navigation.

### [143] [Robots Acquire Manipulation Skills in Seconds from a Single Human Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20033)
*Guangyan Chen,Meiling Wang,Te Cui,Zichen Zhou,Qi Shao,Shalfun Li,Hang Su,Roy Gan,Hao Wang,Mengyin Fu,Yi Yang,Yufeng Yue*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出HOST框架，使机器人能够从单个人类示范视频中在29秒内习得新技能，并保持已有技能不受影响。该方法通过自接地预测级联（任务进度估计→未来观测预测→动作推导）实现技能获取，在62%的成功率下比零样本基线高45%，甚至超越基于50次机器人示范微调的基线，同时所需示范次数减少50倍、技能获取速度快507倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人技能获取方法依赖耗时且昂贵的训练循环，不仅成本高、速度慢，还会侵蚀已掌握的技能。为突破这一瓶颈，作者希望实现快速、低成本的一次性技能习得，同时保证已有技能不被遗忘。

Method: HOST采用三级级联的自接地预测框架：(1) 评估机器人在示范任务中的当前进度；(2) 将下一步进展映射为机器人自身的未来观测；(3) 从预测的观测中推导出具体动作。训练时，通过将机器人轨迹与人类视频映射到共享的任务进度流形上，重新定义每个目标以对齐视频的未来进展，从而完成训练。

Result: 平均29秒即可从单个人类视频习得新技能，成功率62%；比零样本基线高出45%；与基于50次机器人示范微调的基线相比，示范次数减少50倍，技能获取速度快507倍，且不遗忘已有技能。

Conclusion: HOST证明了一种从单个人类视频中快速、高效地获取机器人技能并保持已有技能的可行性，大幅降低了数据和时间成本，为机器人终身学习与技能迁移提供了新范式。

Abstract: The ability to acquire skills rapidly and effortlessly while retaining those already mastered is essential for robots. However, current methods still rely on a cumbersome training-time loop that is costly and slow, while eroding skills already mastered. In this paper, we introduce HOST (Human-to-robot One-Shot Skill AcquisiTion), a framework that enables a robot to acquire skills in seconds from a single human video while retaining previously mastered skills. HOST resolves skill acquisition through a cascade of self-grounded prediction. It first estimates the robot's progress within the demonstrated task, then translates the upcoming progression into the robot's own future observations, and finally derives actions from these predicted observations. This cascade is trained on targets coupled to the video demonstration, obtained by mapping the robot trajectory and the video demonstration onto a shared task progress manifold, then redefining each target to align with the future progression of the video. HOST thereby enables the robot to actively follow the demonstrated procedure and adapt it to the robot's embodiment. HOST acquires novel skills at inference time from a single human video in an average of 29 seconds and achieves a 62% average success rate. It exceeds the zero-shot baseline by 45% while retaining previously mastered skills. HOST even exceeds the baseline fine-tuned on 50 robot demonstrations per task while requiring 50 times fewer demonstrations and acquiring each skill 507 times faster. Additional information about HOST is available on the project website.

</details>


### [144] [ReferTrack: Referring Then Tracking for Embodied Visual Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20061)
*Hanjing Ye,Tianle Zeng,Jiazhao Zhang,Shaoan Wang,Zibo Zhang,Weisi Situ,Yuchen Zhou,Yonggen Ling,Hong Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: ReferTrack提出了一种"先指认后跟踪"的范式，通过前视摄像头先选择目标边界框，再解码跟踪路径点，在EVT-Bench上实现了单视角SOTA性能（成功率89.4%/73.3%/74.1%），并在四足和人形机器人上验证了 Sim-to-Real 迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA策略的CoT推理在抽象空间隐变量中运行，难以监督且与图像空间检测弱对齐，亟需一种显式接地于图像空间的EVT方法。

Method: 提出ReferTrack范式：①从索引边界框集合中选择目标；②基于图像接地决策解码跟踪路径点；③通过滑动窗口队列和TVBI（时间-视角-边界框指示器）令牌注入几何特征保持目标运动线索；④在自定义Refer-QA数据集上协同训练增强目标识别。

Result: 在EVT-Bench上单目标/干扰/歧义跟踪成功率分别为89.4%/73.3%/74.1%，达到单视角SOTA，匹配甚至超越多基线方法；四足和人形机器人真实部署验证了鲁棒的Sim-to-Real迁移。

Conclusion: 将EVT分解为指认和跟踪两个子任务，通过显式图像空间接地有效提升了跟踪鲁棒性，且具有良好的跨平台部署能力。

Abstract: Embodied visual tracking (EVT) requires a mobile agent to continuously follow a specific target described in natural language using only onboard vision. While recent vision-language-action (VLA) policies unify target identification and trajectory planning, their chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning often operates in abstract spatial latents that are difficult to supervise and weakly aligned with explicit image-space detections. To address this, we introduce ReferTrack, a referring-then-tracking paradigm that grounds EVT using a single forward-facing camera. Our model first selects the target from an indexed set of bounding boxes, then decodes tracking waypoints conditioned on this image-grounded decision. To preserve target motion cues over time, ReferTrack maintains a sliding-window queue of previously selected bounding boxes, injecting their geometric features into the visual history via temporal-viewpoint-bbox indicator (TVBI) tokens. We further enhance target identification by co-training on a custom Refer-QA dataset. On EVT-Bench, ReferTrack achieves state-of-the-art single-view performance with success rates of 89.4%, 73.3%, and 74.1% on the single-target, distracted, and ambiguity tracking splits, respectively -- matching or even surpassing several multi-camera baselines on identification-heavy tasks. Finally, real-world deployments on legged and humanoid robots validate its robust sim-to-real transfer capabilities. Code is available at https://github.com/MedlarTea/referTrack.

</details>


### [145] [Extreme-RGMT: Continual Learning of Highly Dynamic Skills for Robust Generalist Humanoid Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20110)
*Yubiao Ma,Han Yu,Kai Guo,Changtai Lv,Zhengquan Mao,Boyang Xing,Xuemei Ren,Dongdong Zheng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出Extreme-RGMT，一个两阶段持续学习框架，用于鲁棒的通用人形机器人控制。该方法先从多源运动数据学习通用运动跟踪基策略，再通过非对称技能获取与能力巩固机制，在保持已有动作性能的同时重点优化高动态运动片段。结合难度感知采样与优势优先轨迹重采样解决高动态运动数据稀缺问题。实验表明，该方法在全身运动跟踪上达到SOTA，能直接执行未见过的各种高动态运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有人形控制器在通用能力与专业技能之间面临权衡：通用运动跟踪策略难以可靠执行罕见的高动态运动，而专业训练又可能退化已习得的行为。需要一种既能获取高动态运动技能又不损害已有日常运动能力的方法。

Method: 两阶段持续学习框架：(1) 从多源运动数据学习通用运动跟踪基策略；(2) 非对称技能获取与能力巩固机制，通过约束已掌握运动的策略漂移并强调高动态困难片段。结合难度感知采样与优势优先轨迹重采样来处理高动态运动数据稀缺和高失败率问题。

Result: 在全身运动跟踪任务上达到SOTA性能，显著提升了对挑战性高动态运动的完成度。控制器能够直接执行未见过的各种高动态运动，包括固定参考和在线惯性动作捕捉输入。

Conclusion: Extreme-RGMT推动了通用全身运动跟踪控制器向人类专家级别的高动态运动能力迈进，解决了通用性与专业性之间的冲突。

Abstract: Humans can progressively acquire highly dynamic motor skills while preserving reliable everyday motor abilities. In contrast, existing humanoid controllers face a trade-off between generalist and specialist capabilities: generalist motion tracking policies struggle to reliably execute rare highly dynamic motions, whereas specialist training can degrade previously acquired behaviors. We introduce Extreme-RGMT, a two-stage continual learning framework for robust generalist humanoid control. The method first learns a generalist motion-tracking base policy from diverse multi-source motion data, then employs an asymmetric skill acquisition and capability consolidation mechanism to constrain policy drift on mastered motions while emphasizing difficult dynamic segments. To address the scarcity of highly dynamic motions, their high failure rates, and the resulting shortage of informative samples, Extreme-RGMT combines difficulty-aware sampling with advantage-prioritized trajectory resampling to emphasize critical segments. Experiments show that Extreme-RGMT achieves state-of-the-art generalist whole-body motion-tracking performance, including substantially improved completion of challenging highly dynamic motions. The resulting controller directly executes diverse unseen highly dynamic motions under fixed references and online inertial motion-capture inputs, advancing generalist whole-body motion-tracking controllers toward highly dynamic motor capabilities at the human-expert level.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么直接用VLM预测抓取但空间感知能力有限，要么将VLM与抓取模型联合训练但需要大量数据和计算资源，难以扩展到多embodiment和复杂场景。

Method: 提出SeededGrasp框架，将高层次语义推理与低层次几何执行解耦：VLM预测种子点作为条件，轻量级抓取生成模型据此输出具体抓取姿态。同时发布了首个多embodiment桌面抓取数据集（超过250万次抓取）。
