Abstract: Practical robotic grasping in complex scenes requires both 3D spatial reasoning and alignment with task-specific requirements. Vision-language models (VLMs) offer a natural way to specify these requirements using language, but existing approaches either use a VLM to predict the grasp directly with limited spatial awareness, or train the VLM together with the grasping model, which requires significantly more data and compute. These limitations impede performance and have prevented scaling to multiple embodiments in complex scenes. We address this by proposing SeededGrasp, a novel data-efficient framework that enables a VLM to predict a seed point to be used as conditioning for a subsequent lightweight grasp-generation model. Our architecture decouples high-level semantic reasoning from low-level geometric execution, enabling multi-embodiment support while bypassing the need for expensive end-to-end training. To enable training such models, we release the first multi-embodiment tabletop grasping dataset comprising over 2.5M grasps in cluttered scenes. Experimental results demonstrate that our approach outperforms existing baselines, achieving 72% success in simulation and 78% in real-world grasping experiments. See our project site for data and code: https://uoft-isl.github.io/seeded-grasp/

### [147] [DINS-IO: Learned Inertial Odometry via Differentiable INS Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20232)
*Hao Qiao,Yan Wang,Jian Kuang,Xiaoji Niu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: DINS-IO提出了一种无需位置标签的惯性里程计学习方法，利用捷联惯导速度递归约束作为自监督损失，仅需少量标注轨迹进行度量校准即可达到或超越全监督方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统学习式惯性里程计依赖动作捕捉、VIO或SLAM提供的高精度位置真值，成本高昂且难以大规模获取。本文旨在消除对位置标签的依赖。

Method: 1) 利用捷联惯导速度递归作为可微分的先验一致性约束，构造滑动窗口最小二乘问题并闭式求解，将残差作为自监督损失；2) 设计高频网络以IMU速率输出体坐标系速度；3) 通过少量标注轨迹对网络进行度量校准，仅更新低秩(LoRA)适配模块。

Result: 在标准基准上，DINS-IO经过自监督预训练和少量标签微调后，性能匹配或超越全监督基线。

Conclusion: 证明了无需位置标签即可有效学习惯性里程计，大幅降低了对昂贵标注数据的依赖，为惯性导航的自监督学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: The training of learned inertial odometry depends on dense, high-precision position ground truth from motion capture, visual-inertial odometry or SLAM, which is costly and hard to acquire at scale. We propose DINS-IO, which learns inertial odometry directly from raw IMU streams without position labels. Our key insight is that the strapdown INS velocity recursion is a strong, fully differentiable consistency prior: the predicted velocity, rotated into the navigation frame, must agree with the integrated specific force up to an unknown initial velocity and a constant accelerometer bias. We cast this constraint as a sliding-window least-squares problem with a globally shared bias, solve it in closed form, and use the solver residual as a self-supervised loss whose gradient flows back to the network through the analytic solution. To supply this per-sample constraint, we design a high-frequency network that emits dense body-frame velocity at the IMU rate. Since the self-supervised network learns consistent motion but its velocity is not yet metrically calibrated, we calibrate it to true metric velocity from a few labeled trajectories by directly supervising the predicted body-frame velocity and adapting only low-rank (LoRA) patches. On standard benchmarks, DINS-IO pretrained self-supervised and fine-tuned with a small fraction of labels matches or surpasses fully supervised baselines.

</details>


### [148] [Courteous Anticipation: Improving Long-Lived Task Planning in Persistent Shared Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20289)
*Md Ridwan Hossain Talukder,Roshan Dhakal,Elizabeth Phillips,Gregory J. Stein*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种礼貌性预期规划方法，通过在任务规划中考虑当前行动对未来所有机器人任务成本的预期影响，利用独立学习的每机器人成本估计器，在持续共享环境中降低长任务序列的总成本，实验显示在家庭和餐厅场景中分别比短视和自私预期规划降低10.43%/4.03%和17.41%/13.24%的成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在共享持久环境的机器人任务规划中，标准规划器缺乏对未来任务的预见性，也不考虑其他机器人的约束，孤立地解决每个任务，导致终端状态增加所有机器人的未来成本，且副作用随任务序列累积，亟需一种能前瞻性地考虑当前行动对未来多机器人任务性能影响的规划方法。

Method: 提出礼貌性预期规划（Courteous Anticipatory Planning），核心包括：1) 基于模型的规划器生成候选计划；2) 通过独立训练的每机器人学习成本估计器，估计每个机器人未来任务的预期成本；3) 选择同时最小化即时成本和所有机器人聚合预期未来成本的计划。这种分式配方避免了组合性的联合 rollout，支持模块化部署。

Result: 在两个持久PDDL领域评估：家庭环境（两机器人，能力相似但责任不同）和餐厅环境（三机器人，能力不同）。在长序列任务中，礼貌性预期规划相比短视规划降低10.43%总成本，相比自私预期规划降低4.03%（两机器人家庭场景）；在餐厅场景中分别降低17.41%和13.24%。

Conclusion: 礼貌性预期规划通过在规划中纳入多机器人间的未来成本预期，有效减少了长任务序列中的累积成本，且其分解式设计具有良好的可扩展性和模块化部署能力。

Abstract: We consider a task planning scenario in which robots sharing a persistent environment are assigned tasks one at a time from a held-out sequence. Standard task planners, lacking foresight of future tasks and inconsiderate of others' constraints, solve each task in isolation, leaving terminal states that increase future cost for all, side effects that compound over lengthy task sequences. To reduce cost over the sequence, a robot must anticipate how its actions now may impact performance on future tasks for all robots sharing the environment. Therefore, we present courteous anticipatory planning, wherein a model-based planner proposes candidate plans and selects the one that jointly minimizes immediate cost and aggregated expected future cost across all robots, estimated via independent per-robot learned estimators. This factored formulation avoids combinatorial joint rollouts and supports modular deployment: adding a robot requires only training its own estimator. We evaluate in two persistent PDDL domains, a home environment with robots that have similar capabilities but different responsibilities, and a restaurant environment where robots' distinct capabilities create states that other robots lack the capability to resolve. During lengthy task sequences, our planner reduces total cost by 10.43% versus myopic and 4.03% versus selfish anticipatory planning in a two-robot home environment and by 17.41% and 13.24%, respectively, in a three-robot restaurant.

</details>

DEED comprises three key components: (1) a data-efficient post-training pipeline with control-frequency alignment, data curation, task-relevant visual highlighting, and reduced VLA dependence; (2) a real-world study of experience-driven refinement, adapted from RECAP via a text-based advantage prefix and a vision-language value function; and (3) a latent-space analysis tool for studying in- and out-of-distribution behavior. *Sebastian Lorca Godoy,Ciera McFarland,Michael Val,Antonio Alvarez Valdivia,Nathaniel Hanson,Margaret McGuinness*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于分布式声学传感的软体藤蔓机器人系统，用于在封闭非结构环境中定位灾难受害者。该系统采用动态SRP-PHAT框架，支持远场DOA估计和近场三维声源定位。实验测试了五种麦克风阵列在三种放置位置和四种机器人构型下的定位精度，并分析了SNR、方向、距离等影响因素。结果表明，仅需三个麦克风从机器人主体外翻后即可实现高精度近场定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软体机器人在封闭非结构化环境中对灾难受害者的定位能力有限，需要一种可靠的外感受感知方案。传统的视觉和触觉传感在烟雾、灰尘或复杂地形下受限，而声学传感具有穿透性和非视距优势，但如何将分布式声学传感集成到形变的软体机器人上仍缺乏系统性研究。

Method: 采用软体藤蔓机器人作为载体，沿其主体嵌入分布式声学传感架构。提出动态SRP-PHAT框架，融合远场DOA估计和近场三维定位。实验设计：五麦克风阵列，三种放置位置（加压体内、内尾部、外壁外），四种机器人构型（直线、双直线、圆形、正弦形），系统评估SNR、声源方向和距离对定位精度的影响。

Result: 1) 麦克风放置位置和机器人构型对定位精度有显著影响；2) 随SNR下降和距离增加，定位精度降低；3) 近场定位可在机器人仅外翻三个麦克风后即达到高精度；4) 分布式声学传感架构在软体机器人任意形变过程中仍能保持有效定位能力。

Conclusion: 基于分布式声学传感的软体藤蔓机器人在封闭非结构化环境中具有可靠的受害者定位潜力。动态SRP-PHAT框架有效支持了机器人形变过程中的声源定位，为软体机器人在搜救等实际应用中提供了新的感知方案。

Abstract: Soft robot exteroception is increasingly being explored for a variety of field applications. In this work, we present a sound-based system for localizing disaster victims in confined and unstructured environments, based on a distributed acoustic sensing architecture embedded along the body of a soft everting vine robot. We propose a dynamic Steered Response Power with Phase Transform framework that supports both far-field direction-of-arrival estimation and near-field three-dimensional source localization as the robot approaches the sound source. To better understand the design and control space related to localizing sound using a soft, shape-morphing robot body, we conduct experiments measuring the accuracy of these methods for a five-microphone array attached to the robot body using three placements relative to the outer membrane of the robot (inside the pressurized body, inside the inner tail, and outside the outer wall) and in four robot configurations (linear, double linear, circular, and sinusoidal). We measure the change in accuracy as the signal-to-noise ratio, the direction of approach, and the distance of the sound source from the center of the array change. Finally, we demonstrate a vine robot growing into an arbitrary shape while carrying microphones along its outer wall, and show that a sound source located with the array's near field can be localized with high accuracy after only three microphones have everted from the robot body. These results highlight the potential of distributed acoustic sensing for reliable victim localization using soft growing robots.

</details>


### [152] [Towards Miniature Humanoid Tele-Loco-Manipulation Using Virtual Reality and Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20399)
*Nicolas Kosanovic,Jordan Dowdy,Jean Chagas Vaz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全尺寸人形机器人的遥操作控制栈（VR上肢+RL下肢）性能强大但成本高昂、难以获取；微型人形机器人更普及但仿生程度低，缺乏类似的控制框架。本文旨在为微型人形机器人构建一套完整的全身遥操作控制栈。

Method: 基于VR实现上肢遥操作，基于强化学习实现下肢平衡与行走控制，构建完整的全身遥操作控制栈，并在ROBOTIS OP3微型人形机器人平台上进行实验验证。

Conclusion: 所开发的系统展现了微型人形机器人在遥操作- locomotion-操作方面的潜力，为低成本、易获取的人形机器人平台提供了可行的全身遥操作方案。

Abstract: Full-sized humanoid robot capabilities have grown exponentially in recent years, aiming towards general-purpose deployment in human environments. A popular control method used by manufacturers utilizes Virtual Reality for upper-body teleoperation and Reinforcement Learning for lower-body balance and locomotion control. As a result, a single remote operator can see, manipulate, and navigate about a real, distant physical environment. This powerful control stack is often relegated to expensive full-sized robots, many of which are inaccessible to the research community. Miniature humanoids are more prevalent, but employ less biomimicry in their design (e.g. fewer sensors, Degrees of Freedom, etc) and lack similar developments. This paper describes a compliant full-body telepresence control stack developed from the ground up for miniature humanoids. Framework experimentation on ROBOTIS OP3 hardware showcases walking at speeds up to 0.45 m/s independent of arm motions. Tele-loco-manipulation is demonstrated via a cube relocation experiment with an expert human operator. On average, the teleoperated system moved 2 different 40 g cubes within 10 mins, walking a total distance of 5 m. Overall, the developed system shows potential for miniature humanoid tele-loco-manipulation.

### [153] [Isaac Sim-to-Real: Reinforcement Learning based Locomotion for Quadrupeds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18135)
*Jordan Dowdy,Jean Chagas Vaz*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于强化学习的四足机器人全身运动控制框架，利用NVIDIA Isaac Sim和Isaac Lab进行训练，实现了零样本的sim-to-real迁移。在Unitree Go1实物机器人上的实验表明，该方法在速度跟踪性能上与自带控制器相当，但具有更强的抗干扰能力，可达到2.0 m/s线速度和1.8 rad/s角速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一个鲁棒的RL运动控制框架，利用NVIDIA Isaac Sim和Isaac Lab进行训练，在Unitree Go1四足机器人上进行零样本（zero-shot）仿真到实物迁移验证。

Result: 在实物硬件上，该策略的速度跟踪性能与Go1自带控制器相当，但具有更强的抗大干扰恢复能力，可实现2.0 m/s线速度和1.8 rad/s角速度。

Conclusion: 所提出的RL框架能够实现零样本的sim-to-real迁移，同时在速度跟踪和抗干扰能力上表现出色，验证了基于Isaac Sim/Isaac Lab训练的策略在实物部署中的有效性。

Abstract: Learning-based approaches to locomotion have risen in popularity in recent years, showing the capability for complex legged locomotion and whole-body control. Reinforcement learning (RL), the primary learning-based approach for locomotion, often utilizes a high-performance simulation tool, providing a controlled and efficient training and development environment. However, policies that perform well in simulation frequently encounter unexpected challenges when deployed on a physical system, known as the sim-to-real gap. This work presents a robust RL locomotion framework capable of whole-body control. The proposed RL framework utilizes Nvidia's new set of simulation tools, Isaac Sim, and its companion RL framework, Isaac Lab, for training, achieving a zero-shot sim-to-real policy. The performance of our policy is validated on physical hardware using the Unitree Go1, with experimental results showing similar velocity tracking performance to the quadruped's integrated controller, with a greater ability to recover from large disturbances, and achieve linear velocities of 2.0 m/s and angular velocities of 1.8 rad/s.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for legged robots is advancing locomotion, demonstrating its ability to adapt to new and challenging terrain. This work explores an RL torque control framework for heavyweight high-torque quadrupeds. The RL framework in this paper can traverse rough terrain and effectively track a desired linear velocity without requiring knowledge of the agent's current velocity. Using Nvidia's Isaac Sim and Isaac Lab, simulation results of the RL torque control policy are shown on the Unitree B1 quadruped, achieving speeds of 3.5 m/s and 1.5 rad/s. In addition, the quadruped can walk up and down stairs without the aid of an exteroceptive sensor.

### [155] [Native Multi-Dimensional Subquadratic Operators via Input Dependent Long Convolutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19378)
*David R. Wessels,Farhad Ramezanghorbani,David W. Romero,Alireza Moradzadeh,Olivia Viessmann,Maksim Zhdanov,John St. John,Ken Janik,David M Knigge,Yucheng Tang,Erik J Bekkers,Saee Gopal Paliwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HyenaND是一种亚二次、全局、输入依赖的算子，通过隐式参数化的多维卷积核直接作用于多维数据的原生几何结构，在基因组学、计算机视觉、医学影像和PDE建模等任务中，纯HyenaND堆栈匹配强注意力基线，而混合配置（HyenaND+注意力）则超越纯注意力和强递归混合模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的亚二次注意力替代方案在处理多维数据时存在妥协：标准卷积缺乏全局感受野和输入依赖性，而递归模型需要将图像、体积和PDE等多维数据光栅化为违反空间结构的临时1D扫描顺序。

Method: 提出HyenaND算子，通过隐式参数化的全局、输入依赖的多维卷积核直接作用于多维数据的原生几何；实现CUDA算子nSubQ，融合FFT-卷积路径将O(L log L)复杂度转化为实际加速。

Result: 在长上下文基因组学、计算机视觉、医学影像和PDE建模任务中，纯HyenaND堆栈匹配强注意力基线；混合HyenaND与注意力的配置性能超越纯注意力和强递归混合模型。

Conclusion: HyenaND作为一种亚二次、全局、输入依赖的多维算子，是注意力机制的有效替代方案，尤其适合处理具有原生几何结构的多维数据。

Abstract: Subquadratic alternatives to attention require compromises when applied to multi-dimensional data: standard convolutions lack global receptive fields and input dependency, while recurrent models require rasterizing data such as images, volumes, and partial differential equation (PDE) into an ad-hoc $1\rm D$ scan order that violates their spatial structure. We introduce \textit{HyenaND}, a subquadratic, global, input-dependent operator that acts directly on the native geometry of multidimensional data through convolutions with implicitly parametrized global, input-dependent multi-dimensional convolutional kernels. Our CUDA implementation, \texttt{nSubQ}, fuses the FFT-convolution path to turn HyenaND's $\mathcal{O}(L \log L)$ scaling into wall-clock speedups. Across long-context genomics, computer vision, medical imaging, and PDE modeling, pure HyenaND stacks match the accuracy of strong attention baselines, while hybrid configurations that interleave HyenaND and attention layers outperform both pure attention and strong recurrence-based hybrids.

</details>


### [156] [Bayesian Wind Tunnels for Model Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19379)
*Siddhartha R Dalal,Vishal Misra,Abhay Parekh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现小型Transformer（2.8M参数）能在受控环境中实现精确贝叶斯模型选择（区分对合与三循环，熵偏差0.01比特），但存在尖锐的感知边界：当判别统计量依赖模运算时，整数token成功而透明符号失败，且该边界在参数扩大112倍后依然存在。前沿LLM表现出定性贝叶斯行为但校准差距约55倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作证明Transformer能在固定假设类内执行精确贝叶斯滤波，但能否进行贝叶斯模型选择（从数据中识别正确假设类）尚不清楚。本文旨在探究Transformer在受控环境中实现模型选择的能力及其边界条件。

Method: 设计"模型选择贝叶斯风洞"——一种可获得真实后验的受控环境，使用固定点自由对合（f(f(x))=x）作为纯关系判别特征。实验包括：2.8M参数Transformer在整数token与透明符号上的模型选择；非嵌套比较（对合vs三循环）；模运算（模加、模乘）条件下的感知边界测试；参数缩放实验（2.8M到316M）；以及前沿LLM的探测实验。

Result: 1) 2.8M参数Transformer在对合识别任务上达到0.01比特熵偏差；2) 非嵌套比较（对合vs三循环）的类后验MAE低于0.001；3) 模运算条件下整数token成功而透明符号完全失败，该边界在112倍参数缩放后依然存在；4) 固定重标定的透明符号成功（0.009比特MAE），说明稳定语义而非整数身份才是关键；5) 前沿LLM表现出定性贝叶斯行为但校准差距约55倍。

Conclusion: Transformer能够进行纯关系的贝叶斯模型选择，但存在尖锐的感知边界：需要算术运算的判别任务依赖稳定语义来编译电路。标头子任务诊断将失败定位在标头反转与算术的组合而非标头解析本身。这些发现揭示了Transformer在统计推理中的能力与局限。

Abstract: Prior work has shown that transformers can perform exact Bayesian filtering within a fixed
  hypothesis class. Can they also perform Bayesian model selection -- identifying the correct
  hypothesis class from data? We introduce model-selection Bayesian wind tunnels: controlled
  environments where ground-truth posteriors over hypothesis classes are available in closed
  form. Using fixed-point-free involutions -- whose defining property f(f(x))=x is purely
  relational -- a 2.8M-parameter transformer achieves 0.01-bit entropy agreement with the
  Bayesian optimum (3 seeds), with both integer tokens and opaque symbols whose meanings
  change every episode. This extends to non-nested comparisons: involutions vs. 3-cycles
  (where neither class is a subset of the other) achieve class-posterior MAE under 0.001,
  demonstrating genuine model selection beyond simplicity/subset bias. We then identify a
  sharp perceptual access condition: when the discriminative statistic requires arithmetic --
  modular addition (rotations) or multiplication (f(x)=cx mod p) -- model selection succeeds
  with integer tokens but fails completely with opaque symbols, and this boundary persists
  under 112x scaling (2.8M to 316M parameters). A stationarity control confirms the operative
  factor: opaque tokens with a fixed relabeling succeed (0.009-bit MAE), showing that stable
  semantics, not integer identity, enable circuit compilation. Header subtask diagnostics
  localize the failure to the composition of header inversion with arithmetic rather than
  header parsing itself. Probing frontier LLMs on the same tasks shows qualitative Bayesian
  behavior but a large calibration gap (~55x), measured through lossy probes and therefore
  directional rather than exact.

</details>


### [157] [CruiseBench: A Real-Flight-Aligned N-CMAPSS Benchmark for Engine RUL Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19380)
*Pu Cheng,Qiang Miao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对N-CMAPSS数据集因全航段时间序列复杂导致RUL评估控制不足的问题，提出CruiseBench——基于巡航阶段的RUL基准。通过CPM-N-CMAPSS掩码提取巡航区间，固定特征输入（排除虚拟传感器等）、保持原生分辨率窗口、应用数据集级RUL上限。实验表明TSMixer表现最优（RMSE=3.4±1.71），消融研究验证了航段选择、时间下采样方法及RUL阈值的影响。CruiseBench提供可复现的RUL模型比较子基准，CPM-N-CMAPSS为迁移学习与域适应研究提供阶段特定数据基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: N-CMAPSS数据集虽增加了真实性（记录完整航段时间序列），但全航段数据量庞大且退化信号与运行工况变化纠缠，导致预处理选择复杂、RUL模型性能直接对比困难，缺乏评估控制力。现有C-MAPSS基准在N-CMAPSS上不适用，亟需一个可控、可复现的RUL子基准。

Method: 1) 提出CPM-N-CMAPSS掩码，利用共同高度法识别9个可访问子数据集中每个循环的巡航阶段区间；2) 构建CruiseBench基准协议：仅使用情景描述符与实测传感器作为输入，排除虚拟传感器、健康参数及辅助元数据，保持原生分辨率时间窗口，应用数据集级RUL上限（cap）；3) 以LSTM、GRU、TCN、TSMixer作为基线模型进行实验与消融研究。

Result: 在CruiseBench-eta5-W256-S10设定下，TSMixer取得最低平均RMSE（3.4±1.71）和最低Saxena分数（(2.50±2.99)×10⁴）。消融研究显示航段选择（巡航vs.全航段）、时间下采样方法及RUL-cap阈值均显著影响结果。

Conclusion: CruiseBench通过固定巡航阶段协议提供了一个可复现的RUL模型对比子基准，CPM-N-CMAPSS为后续迁移学习与域适应研究提供了阶段特定的数据基础。

Abstract: Remaining useful life (RUL) prediction estimates how long an engine can continue safe operation and is central to maintenance planning. N-CMAPSS extends C-MAPSS by simulating run-to-failure aero-engine trajectories using recorded real-flight profiles and retaining complete within-flight time series rather than cycle-level snapshots. However, this added realism reduces evaluation control because full-flight records increase data volume and entangle degradation cues with operating-regime variation, complicating preprocessing choices and direct comparisons of RUL modeling performance. To mitigate this issue, this paper proposes CruiseBench, a cruise-stage RUL benchmark derived from N-CMAPSS. It introduces CPM-N-CMAPSS (Cruising-Period Mask for N-CMAPSS), a mask artifact that stores cycle-local cruising intervals identified by the common-altitude method for the nine accessible subdatasets. CruiseBench applies a fixed protocol to the masked rows, using scenario descriptors and measured sensors as inputs while excluding virtual sensors, health parameters, and auxiliary metadata from the feature tensor, preserving native-resolution windows, and applying dataset-wise RUL caps. Experiments with LSTM, GRU, TCN, and TSMixer provide baseline results for this setting. Under CruiseBench-eta5-W256-S10, TSMixer obtains the lowest average RMSE, $3.4\pm1.71$, and Saxena score, $(2.50\pm2.99)\times 10^{4}$. Ablation studies show that flight-stage selection, temporal downscaling method, and RUL-cap threshold affect reported results. With its fixed cruise-stage protocol, CruiseBench provides a reproducible sub-benchmark for controlled RUL model comparison and CPM-N-CMAPSS provides a stage-specific data foundation for future transfer-learning and domain-adaptation studies.

</details>


### [158] [Air Quality Arena: A Large-Scale Multi-Region Ground Monitoring Dataset and Benchmark for Air Quality Forecasting with Time-Series Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19381)
*Rishi Bharadwaj,Manik Gupta,Pandarasamy Arjunan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了Air Quality Arena (AQA)，一个大规模、多国家、多污染物的空气质量基准测试平台，包含AQA-Data数据集和AQA-Bench基准，覆盖7个国家4大洲6种主要污染物的14,000多条站点-污染物时间序列。实验表明，时序基础模型（TSFMs）在零样本预测中优于经典基线方法，其中采用跨模态架构（利用视觉基础模型进行时序预测）的模型表现最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有空气质量预测基准在地理范围、污染物覆盖方面存在局限，且未能评估最新一代时序基础模型（TSFMs）在大规模真实世界数据上的表现。

Method: 构建了包含6种主要污染物、横跨7个国家4大洲、超过14,000条站点-污染物序列的三年期数据集（AQA-Data），并设计基准测试（AQA-Bench）；对11种前沿时序基础模型和经典基线方法进行短期空气质量预测性能评估。

We present Air Quality Arena (AQA), a large scale multi-country and multi-pollutant dataset (AQA-Data) and benchmark (AQA-Bench) to address this gap. Our results demonstrate that TSFMs are effective zero-shot forecasters and consistently outperform classical baselines, with our top-performing model employing a cross-modal architecture that leverages a vision foundation model for time series forecasting. Method: 将FCIL重新解释为统一的多任务学习问题，将客户端和任务更新表示为共享参数空间中的适应向量。提出SUM框架，在服务端聚合过程中对适应向量执行几何手术：空间SUM缓解每轮内的客户端间干扰，因果在线时间SUM消除跨任务干扰。该方法仅需服务端操作，不增加客户端计算、通信或内存开销。

Abstract: Real-world intelligent systems often require both distributed collaboration across data-isolated clients and continual adaptation to evolving tasks. This setting naturally gives rise to Federated Class Incremental Learning (FCIL), which combines Federated Learning (FL) and Continual Learning (CL). However, their combination introduces two coupled sources of interference: spatial interference from heterogeneous clients and temporal interference from sequential tasks, jointly leading to Spatial-Temporal Catastrophic Forgetting (ST-CF). Existing approaches typically address spatial and temporal interference with separate mechanisms, often incurring additional client-side computation or communication, while leaving directional interactions among updates during aggregation unregulated. In this paper, we reinterpret FCIL as a unified multi-task learning problem, where both client and task updates are represented as adaptation vectors in a shared parameter space. Based on this view, we propose Unified Geometric Surgery on Spatio-Temporal Adaptation Vectors (SUM), a purely server-side framework that performs geometric surgery on adaptation vectors during aggregation. Spatial SUM mitigates client-level interference within each round, while causal online temporal SUM removes cross-task interference over time without additional client-side computation, communication, or memory beyond standard federated training. Empirically, SUM achieves up to 22% improvement over prior FCIL methods across diverse vision and language benchmarks while remaining robust to unreliable clients and maintaining computational efficiency.

### [162] [Building Fast, Evaluating Slow: Pipeline Choices Dominate Autointerpretability Score Variance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19386)

Method: 在四种指标（simulation, detection, fuzzing, purity）、两个模型（Pythia-160M, Apertus-8B）和四个方法学变化轴上进行了系统实验，通过方差分解量化方法方差与架构方差的相对大小，并分析top-k排序稳定性。

Abstract: Cross-paper comparison of sparse autoencoder (SAE) interpretability often relies on autointerpretability scores. In this evaluation pipeline, a language model (LM) explains each feature, and another LM scores the explanation. For these comparisons to be meaningful, scores must reflect stable properties of the features rather than confounding aspects of the evaluation pipeline. Through systematic experiments across four metrics (simulation, detection, fuzzing, purity), two models (Pythia-160M, Apertus-8B), and four axes of methodological variation, we show that this assumption does not hold. Specifically, we find that R1) methodological variance collectively exceeds architectural variance across all metrics and tested models; R2) each metric exhibits a distinct instability profile, with detection being the most stable and fuzzing unreliable across all conditions; R3) top-k feature rankings do not stay consistent across corpus and draw conditions, masking per-feature instability behind stable mean scores; a failure that cannot be detected by monitoring explanation similarity alone. These findings suggest that cross-paper comparisons based on autointerpretability scores may reflect pipeline differences rather than architectural differences, with implications for the ongoing debate on SAE utility. More broadly, unreliable evaluation slows progress in interpretability research at a time when reliable tools for understanding AI systems are needed. To support evaluation, we contribute a variance decomposition approach, a Stability Check, and a Minimum Reporting Checklist.

### [163] [Scale-Aware Learning of Chaotic Dynamics on Unstructured Meshes via Binned Spectral Losses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19387)
*Kanad Sen,Romit Maulik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对非结构化网格上的高维非线性混沌动力系统代理建模，提出了基于图拉普拉斯频段的频谱损失函数，通过切比雪夫多项式近似和多层级图架构（GLEAM）实现可扩展的频带功率匹配，在湍流预测任务中有效提升了长期 rollout 保真度和统计不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统频带频谱损失函数（如binned spectral loss）依赖于结构化网格上的傅里叶分解，无法直接应用于非结构化网格。然而许多实际物理系统（如湍流）使用非结构化网格进行离散化，缺乏规范傅里叶基。因此需要一种能够在不规则网格上进行频谱监督的代理建模方法，以保持长期rollout的尺度结构。

Method: (1) 将傅里叶频带替换为图拉普拉斯频带，利用图拉普拉斯特征空间构建频带功率匹配的类比； (2) 提出可扩展的切比雪夫多项式图滤波器近似，避免显式特征分解的高昂代价； (3) 提出GLEAM（Graph Laplacian Energy Alignment for Meshes），在多层级图架构中实现保留子空间的尺度感知监督，在粗-细层级间进行正则化。

Result: 在非结构化网格的湍流预测任务中，相比确定性基线方法，所提出的频谱损失显著提升了长期rollout保真度，并更好地保持了统计不变量。

Conclusion: 图拉普拉斯频带损失为非结构化网格上的非线性动力系统代理建模提供了一种有效的频谱监督机制，切比雪夫近似和GLEAM多层级策略在保持精度的同时显著降低了计算成本，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Surrogate modeling for high-dimensional nonlinear dynamical systems that exhibit chaos requires mechanisms that preserve not only pointwise accuracy but also the scale-dependent structure of physical fields. Bandwise spectral power losses, such as the binned spectral loss function, provide such supervision on structured grids, where Fourier modes define a standard frequency decomposition. On irregular meshes, however, no canonical Fourier basis exists, and spectral representations must be constructed from graph operators induced by mesh connectivity and geometry. In this study, we extend the binned spectral power loss for application to unstructured-mesh surrogate modeling of nonlinear dynamical systems. This is obtained by replacing Fourier bands with graph-Laplacian frequency bands, and we provide scalable Chebyshev and multilevel approximations for improving long-horizon rollout fidelity. In its full-spectrum form, our approach uses graph Laplacian eigenspaces to provide a graph analogue of Fourier band-power matching, but incurs the high cost of spectral decomposition. As a scalable approximation, we replace exact band projectors with sparse Chebyshev polynomial graph filters, avoiding explicit eigendecomposition. When utilizing multilevel graph architectures, we introduce Graph Laplacian Energy Alignment for Meshes (GLEAM), which applies retained-subspace scale-aware supervision across graph hierarchies so that coarse and fine representations are regularized during autoregressive rollout. Our results show that the proposed spectral losses improve long-horizon rollout fidelity and preserve statistical invariants for the forecasting of turbulent flows on unstructured meshes, compared to deterministic baselines.

We consider three surrogates. The first two map the material and source fields directly to the flux, one using an FNO and one using a UNO. ### [165] [The Orthogonalized Read Is a Removable Training Scaffold for Recurrent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19390)
*Keston Aquino-Michaels*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现mLSTM的正交化读取（Newton-Schulz迭代）并非改善记忆，而是通过重新调节学习问题来加速训练逃逸，其效果可被精确的递归最小二乘读取（Mesa层）复现，且可被安全移除；研究进一步表明，该任务中的涌现现象源于对逐渐累积结构的截断度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 正交化mLSTM记忆矩阵在读取时（五次Newton-Schulz迭代，端到端训练）显著提升了 noisy associative recall 的性能。作者希望探究这一改进的本质机制：它真的改善了记忆，还是另有原因？

Method: 通过三个性质（自洽性、均匀性、可移除性）建立论证。自洽性：精确的递归最小二乘读取（Mesa层）可复现效果，而straight-through、delta-rule写入、冻结随机键、普通归一化均失败。均匀性：在learning-rate x hardness网格上，正交化读取使逃逸危险率提高约6倍，且与难度无关。可移除性：对失败模型在推理时应用无改善，逃逸触发后退火可得完全正常模型。进一步分析逃逸危险率的热/噪声定律（学习率弹性+3.0，梯度噪声弹性-1.65），并直接解码记忆状态。

Result: 正交化读取并非记忆改善，而是重新调节了学习问题：在训练平台期，它通过改善梯度条件加速了逃逸。原始词汇量96的结果实为大批次噪声条件而非容量条件。失败模型约一半关联以线性可恢复形式存在——平台期本质上是半写存储上的读取失败。

Conclusion: 两点超越性结论：1）用于架构选择的召回基准部分衡量的可训练性；2）该系统可作为“涌现”的完整仪器化模式生物——尖锐的行为阈值源自对逐渐累积结构的截断度量。

Abstract: A recent report finds that orthogonalizing the mLSTM memory matrix at read time (five Newton-Schulz iterations, trained through) substantially improves noisy associative recall. The effect replicates, but it is not a memory improvement. Training on this task is a long chance plateau followed by a sharp escape, and the orthogonalized read acts by re-conditioning the learning problem during the plateau. Three properties establish this. It must be self-consistent: an exact recursive least-squares read (the Mesa layer) reproduces it, while straight-through halves, delta-rule writes, frozen random keys, and plain normalization all fail. It is uniform: across a learning-rate x hardness grid it multiplies the escape hazard roughly six-fold with no detectable hardness dependence, widening the workable learning-rate corridor that narrows for the baseline. And it is removable: applied to failed models at inference it rescues none, and annealed away on an escape-triggered schedule it leaves numerically stock mLSTMs at full accuracy. Much of the published gain needs no architecture at all -- solved-rate at a fixed budget measures escape hazard, which follows a heat/noise law (learning-rate elasticity +3.0, gradient-noise elasticity -1.65) under which the original vocab-96 result is a large-batch noise condition rather than a capacity one. Decoding the memory state directly shows failed models carry roughly half their associations in linearly recoverable form: the plateau is a readout failure over half-written storage. Two conclusions travel beyond the intervention: recall benchmarks used for architecture selection partly measure trainability, and the system is a fully instrumented model organism of "emergence," in which a sharp behavioral threshold demonstrably arises from a censored metric over gradually accumulating structure.

</details>

*Ashutosh Tripathi,Surya Deep Singh,Pranab Sahoo,Sriparna Saha*

TL;DR: LAARA是一种基于Fisher信息矩阵的动态秩分配框架，无需搜索即可为不同Transformer层自适应分配适配器秩，在GLUE和MathInstruct基准上以更少参数匹配或超越LoRA等SOTA方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低秩适配方法（如LoRA）对所有Transformer层使用相同的适配器秩，忽略了各层在微调中异构的适配需求，导致资源分配次优。

Method: LAARA框架包含四个关键组件：投影维度归一化、对数压缩、混合适配器重要性估计以及投票变化阻尼机制，利用训练中计算的光量级对角Fisher估计来动态分配秩，无需昂贵的搜索过程。

Result: 在GLUE和MathInstruct基准上，LAARA以显著更少的可训练参数，一致地匹配或超越了LoRA、AdaLoRA、DyLoRA和Bitfit等流行方法。

Conclusion: Fisher引导的秩分配为自适应参数高效微调提供了原则性且有效的理论基础，证明了按层重要性分配计算资源的范式是更优的微调策略。

Abstract: Low-Rank Adaptation is widely used for parameter-efficient fine-tuning, yet existing methods typically assign the same adapter rank to every transformer layer despite their heterogeneous adaptation requirements. In this work, we show theoretically and empirically that uniform rank allocation is fundamentally suboptimal. Motivated by this observation, we propose LAARA (Layer Aware Adaptive Rank Allocation framework), a search-free framework that dynamically allocates ranks using lightweight diagonal Fisher estimates computed during training. LAARA combines projection-wise normalization, logarithmic compression, blended adapter importance estimation, and a vote-to-change dampening mechanism to produce stable and efficient rank adaptation. Experiments on GLUE and MathInstruct benchmark demonstrate that LAARA consistently matches or outperforms popular state of the art approaches such as LoRA, AdaLoRA, DyLoRA, and Bitfit while using significantly fewer trainable parameters. Our results show that Fisher-guided rank allocation provides a principled and effective foundation for adaptive parameter-efficient fine-tuning. The code is publicly available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/LAARA-D305/LAARA.py

</details>


### [167] [Predicting Groundwater Arsenic Concentrations Using Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19392)

Abstract: Arsenic contamination in groundwater presents a longstanding public health crisis in the United States, especially for households depending on private wells. Accurate and spatially informed prediction of arsenic concentration is vital to identify high-risk areas and focus mitigation efforts. However, there is a lack of generalizable models for representing continuous variation in arsenic concentrations across regions. Specifically, we use a variety of techniques including kNearest Neighbors (k-NN) and Geographic Information Systems (GIS) to join arsenic measurement points from across the United States by location. Building on this dataset, we evaluate a diverse suite of machine learning models, including tree-based ensemble approaches, multilayer perceptrons, and spatially aware graph neural networks (GNN). Our findings show that while gradient-boosted trees are still considered state-of-the-art in the field of tabular data, GNNs are able to further account for spatial dependence to match or outperform the results of gradient-boosted trees. These results demonstrate that graph-based and spatially informed learning can enhance environmental prediction and provide a foundation for improved groundwater risk mapping and monitoring.

### [168] [Decodable but Not Detectable: A Leakage Fingerprint for Near-OOD Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19393)
*Vishnu Bindu Balachandran*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现一个面向文档的基于扰动的OOD检测基准存在标签泄露问题：被标记为"OOD"的类别实际上是模型训练过的类别，导致AUROC仅0.326（低于随机水平0.5）。删除该类别并重新训练后，AUROC提升至0.911。作者将这种泄露特征提炼为一种"泄露指纹"（监督可解码性接近完美，无监督检测崩溃），并在52个控制实验设置中验证了诊断方法。后续对24个标准OOD基准对的审核仅触发一个告警。在修正协议下，扰动信号可解码但不可检测。本文贡献在于提供了修正协议和有效的泄露诊断工具，而非新的OOD方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发现基于扰动的OOD检测器在文档基准上的AUROC异常低（0.326），远低于随机水平0.5，进一步分析发现基准存在标签泄露——被归为"OOD"的类别实际上是训练集的一部分，导致检测器因正确识别这些样本为"熟悉"而被错误惩罚。

Method: 1) 识别泄露来源：被标记为OOD的类别实际在训练集中；2) 删除泄露类别并重新训练35个模型（两个域）验证效果；3) 提出"泄露指纹"：监督可解码性AUROC接近1，无监督检测AUROC低于0.65；4) 在52个控制设置（20泄露/32干净）中验证诊断方法（嵌入空间灵敏18/20，特指31/32）；5) 对24个标准OOD基准对进行野外审核；6) 在修正协议下分析扰动信号的可解码性与可检测性；7) 提供理论解释并撤回早期发现的虚假相关。

Result: 泄露类别删除后AUROC从0.326提升至0.911；泄露指纹在52个控制实验中灵敏度18/20，特指31/32（匹配的fit-set-exclusion控制完美20/20）；24个标准基准对中仅触发一个告警（CIFAR-100 vs CIFAR-10）；修正协议下扰动信号监督可解码AUROC达0.87-1.00，但无监督检测器无法检测；扰动方法未优于普通马氏距离。

Conclusion: 本文核心贡献是揭示了广泛使用的OOD检测基准中的标签泄露问题，提出了有效的泄露诊断工具，并提供了修正后的实验协议。研究强调了对基准完整性进行系统性检查的重要性，提醒社区注意数据泄露对OOD检测评估的潜在影响。

Abstract: While auditing a perturbation-based OOD detector on a document benchmark, we recorded an AUROC of 0.326 -- well below the 0.5 chance level. The cause is a benchmark leak: the designated "OOD" class is one the model was trained on, so its examples sit inside the in-distribution fit set and the detector is penalized for correctly ranking them as familiar. Deleting the class and retraining 35 models across two domains raises the score to 0.911. We distill the contamination into a leak fingerprint -- near-perfect supervised decodability (AUROC approximately 1) coupled with unsupervised detection collapsed below 0.65 -- and validate it on a controlled battery of 52 settings (20 leaked, 32 clean) across ResNet-50 and ViT-B/16 on CIFAR-10/100, achieving sensitivity 18/20 and specificity 31/32 in embedding space; the matched fit-set-exclusion controls are perfect at 20/20. An in-the-wild audit of 24 standard near/far OOD benchmark pairs fires on exactly one (the intrinsically hard CIFAR-100 vs CIFAR-10 pair) and on no far-OOD pair, confirming specificity and that standard cross-dataset construction is clean. Under the corrected protocol, perturbation signals are decodable but not detectable: a supervised reader recovers the OOD signal (AUROC 0.87-1.00) while no unsupervised detector does, and the perturbation method does not improve on plain Mahalanobis distance. We provide a theoretical account of why and, for transparency, retract an earlier circular correlation. The contributions are a corrected protocol and a validated leak diagnostic, not a new OOD method.

</details>


### [169] [Cross-Subject Semantic Decoding with Shared-Space Alignment for Generalized Neural Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19394)
*Ji-Hoon Heo,Aleksandra Joanna Wisniewska,Seo-Hyun Lee,Seong-Whan Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种跨被试语义解码框架，通过共享反应模型将多被试的神经响应对齐到共享潜空间，并训练解码器预测上下文语义嵌入，从而提升对新被试的泛化能力。实验表明该方法在跨被试泛化上优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 侵入式神经记录中，不同被试的电极配置、解剖结构和神经信号模式存在显著差异，导致跨被试泛化困难。现有方法难以有效解决这一个体间变异性问题。

Method: 基于ECoG数据，首先利用共享反应模型（Shared Response Model）估计多被试的共享潜空间，将神经响应对齐；然后训练解码器将对齐后的神经表征映射到上下文语义嵌入空间；对新被试，仅需估计其到共享空间的投影矩阵，直接使用预训练解码器，无需重新训练。

Result: 该方法在所有评估设置下持续优于基线方法，且从源被试到新被试测试的性能下降幅度更小，表明跨被试泛化能力得到显著改善。

Conclusion: 将神经活动对齐到共享潜空间并在语义嵌入空间中进行解码，能够有效减少被试特异性差异、捕捉共享的刺激相关表征，是提升跨被试泛化能力的有效策略。

Abstract: Generalizing across subjects remains challenging in invasive neural recordings because electrode configurations, anatomical structures, and neural signal patterns vary substantially across individuals. To investigate such inter-subject variability, we propose a cross-subject semantic decoding framework that aligns neural responses to speech perception from multiple subjects into a shared latent space and learns a mapping from the aligned neural representations to contextual embeddings. More specifically, using electrocorticography data collected during natural language comprehension, we estimate the shared space using the shared response model and train a decoder to predict contextual semantic embeddings from projected neural responses. For a held-out subject, we estimate a subject-specific projection into the predefined shared space, and directly apply the pretrained decoder without any retraining. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed framework consistently outperforms baseline methods across evaluation settings and exhibits a reduced performance drop from source subject to held-out subject testing, indicating improved cross-subject generalization. These results suggest that aligning neural activity into a shared latent space, while decoding in a semantic embedding space, provides an effective strategy for improving cross-subject generalization by reducing subject-specific differences in neural responses while effectively capturing shared stimulus-related representations.

### [170] [From Trajectories to Prefixes: Reusing Teacher Trajectories via Replayed Prefixes and Online Continuation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19395)
*Yihan Wang,Zhong Guan,Haoran Sun,Jiale Huang,Likang Wu,Hongke Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Prefix-GRPO是一种强化学习框架，通过将教师轨迹分解为重放对齐的前缀查询和在线延续，并结合前缀令牌的剪裁策略更新，有效提升了小模型在长时域交互任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接从小模型蒸馏教师轨迹会将丰富的多轮交互行为简化为单次模仿目标，在长时域环境中效率低下，因为早期决策会影响后续状态和奖励。

Method: 将教师轨迹分解为前缀查询和在线延续；在环境中重放前缀以恢复有效中间状态；学生模型继续在线交互并获取奖励；对重放前缀中的历史助手令牌应用剪裁策略更新，并使用策略蒸馏的SFT检查点估计其旧对数概率。

Result: 在TextCraft、BabyAI和ALFWorld基准上，Prefix-GRPO相比蒸馏和标准RL基线显著提升了小模型性能；消融实验表明，没有显式前缀令牌优化的情况下，仅靠重放是不够的。

Conclusion: Prefix-GRPO通过统一的策略优化框架统一了前缀学习和延续学习，为小模型作为交互智能体骨干提供了更有效的训练方案。

Abstract: Small language models are attractive backbones for interactive agents, but direct distillation from strong teacher trajectories often turns rich multi-turn behavior into one-shot imitation targets. This is inefficient in long-horizon environments, where early decisions shape later states and rewards. We propose Prefix-GRPO, a reinforcement learning framework that decomposes teacher trajectories into replay-aligned prefix queries and online continuations. Each prefix is replayed in the environment to recover a valid intermediate state, after which the student continues online interaction and receives task reward. Unlike response-only GRPO, Prefix-GRPO also applies clipped policy updates to historical assistant tokens inside the replayed prefix, using a policy-distilled SFT checkpoint to estimate their old log-probabilities. This unifies prefix learning and continuation learning within the same policy-optimization form. Experiments on TextCraft, BabyAI, and ALFWorld show that Prefix-GRPO improves small-model agents over distillation and standard RL baselines, while ablations show that replay alone is insufficient without explicit prefix-token optimization. The implementation and reproduction scripts are available at https://github.com/HappynessI/Prefix_GRPO.

</details>


### [171] [Memory Merge DQN: Sensitivity Weighted Target Updates for Stable Value Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19397)
*Adrian Ly,Richard Dazeley,Peter Vamplew,Sunil Aryal,Francisco Cruz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Memory Merge DQN，一种通过基于Q值敏感性的网络参数合并来替代硬拷贝更新的目标网络机制，在Atari环境中相比DQN、Averaged DQN等方法取得了更优的最终性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准DQN的硬拷贝目标网络更新方式存在权衡：固定目标网络提供短期稳定性，但每次硬更新会突然替换参数并丢弃近期参数历史，导致自举目标突变，可能移除后期仍有用的价值函数结构。

Method: 提出Memory Merge DQN，维护近期历史在线网络副本的短记忆，基于Q值敏感性（而非Fisher信息）进行网络参数合并来构建目标网络，同时使用近因先验使合并后的目标接近最新在线参数。

Result: 在Atari环境上与DQN、Averaged DQN、层归一化DQN及PQN（梯度裁剪）对比，Memory Merge DQN获得最多第一名的最终性能结果，击败DQN、Averaged DQN和PQN，在多个游戏中带来显著提升。

Conclusion: 选择性合并近期参数权重和历史可以提升DQN智能体的稳定性和最终性能，目标网络设计是长视界价值学习中保留有用价值函数结构的重要机制。

Abstract: Deep Q-networks use target networks to stabilise bootstrapped value learning, but the standard hard copy update also introduces a tradeoff. Holding the target network fixed, improves short term stability, yet each hard update abruptly replaces the target parameters with the newest online network and discards recent parameter history. This can produce sudden changes in the bootstrap target and may remove value function structure that remains useful later in training. This paper introduces Memory Merge DQN, a target network update mechanism that maintains a short memory of recent historical online network copies and constructs the target network by merging network parameters based on the Q-value sensitivity rather than copying only the newest online network. Memory Merge gives greater influence to parameters that remain locally important for current Q-value behaviour, while using a recency prior to keep the merged target close to the latest online parameters. The method is inspired by Fisher Weight Model Merging, but uses Q-value sensitivity rather than Fisher information as the weighting signal. This paper evaluates Memory Merge DQN on Atari environments against DQN, Averaged DQN, DQN with layer normalisation, and PQN (with gradient clipping). The results show that Memory Merge DQN is highly competitive and it achieves the largest number of first place final performance results among the evaluated methods, beats DQN, Averaged DQN, and PQN (with gradient clipping), and produces substantial gains in several games where preserving useful value-function parameters appears beneficial. These findings suggest that selectively merging recent parameter weights and history can improve the stability and final performance of DQN agents, and that target network design is an important mechanism for preserving useful value function structure during long horizon value learning.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两种正则化方式：1）利用离线数据进行监督正则化；2）利用离线训练的参考策略进行策略约束。在OOD基准上比较离线-only训练、标准在线RL以及上述混合方法。

Abstract: It is commonly observed that online reinforcement learning (RL) produces better-performing strategies than offline methods across a broad range of performance measures. In particular, RL-trained policies exhibit stronger out-of-distribution (OOD) behavior, where models trained only with imitation learning approaches often struggle. A recent study introduced an OOD-focused benchmark and reported that RL-trained vision-language-action (VLA) policies achieve noticeably better OOD performance and slightly better in-distribution (IND) performance than their counterparts trained with supervised fine-tuning (SFT). In this work, we investigate whether hybrid offline-online training can combine the advantages of both approaches. Specifically, we study RL methods regularized by offline supervision via either offline data or an offline-trained reference policy. We evaluate these approaches on the OOD benchmark and compare them with both offline-only training and standard RL. Our results show that although offline training achieves limited OOD performance by itself, incorporating offline supervision into RL preserves strong OOD capability while substantially improving training efficiency. In particular, the guided methods reach performance close to that of standard RL while requiring roughly half of the training budget. Rather than producing a trade-off between speed and OOD performance, the hybrid approach retains strong OOD capability while achieving this efficiency gain. Project page: https://alstar8.github.io/offline-supervision-vla-rl

TL;DR: 本文对共识分割进行了严谨的数学推导和实证验证，发现STAPLE在常见医学影像条件下退化为阈值化多数投票、存在95%的EM次优性并因类别不平衡而崩溃，而多数投票是出人意料的强基线；同时，深度共识模型表明结合图像信息可使问题变得可解，共形预测可提供正式的不确定性保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前医学影像共识分割领域过度推崇STAPLE等复杂方法，但对其数学基础和实际性能缺乏严格的审视，作者旨在从第一性原理出发揭示这些方法的真实表现，为从业者提供更可靠的方法选择依据。

Method: 从生成模型、EM算法、Van Leemput边缘化分析、可辨识性条件、Spatial STAPLE到深度变分公式，逐步建立数学基础，并通过受控实验验证每个理论预测。

Result: STAPLE在常见条件下退化为阈值化多数投票，EM算法存在95%的次优性，在类别不平衡场景下完全失效；多数投票作为非参数化基线方法表现优异；深度共识模型结合图像信息后问题变得可解；共形预测可提供实用的不确定性保证。

Conclusion: 呼吁从业者批判性地评估共识方法而非默认使用STAPLE，多数投票是常被忽视的强基线，结合图像信息的深度共识模型和共形预测为更原则性的方法提供了理论和实证基础。

Abstract: This paper provides a rigorous, self-contained investigation of consensus segmentation. We derive the mathematical foundations from first principles -- the generative model, EM algorithm, Van Leemput's marginalization analysis, identifiability conditions, Spatial STAPLE, and deep variational formulations -- and validate each theoretical prediction through controlled experiments. The central finding is sobering: under common conditions, STAPLE reduces to thresholded majority voting, suffers 95% EM suboptimality, and collapses under class imbalance. These are not edge cases but typical scenarios in medical imaging. Majority voting -- simple, non-parametric, and robust -- is a surprisingly strong baseline that the field has perhaps too hastily dismissed in favor of more "sophisticated" methods. At the same time, the deep consensus model demonstrates that the consensus problem is not inherently difficult -- it becomes tractable when the image is used alongside the labels. And conformal prediction shows that formal uncertainty guarantees are achievable and practical. We hope this work encourages practitioners to critically evaluate their consensus methods rather than applying STAPLE by default, and provides the mathematical and empirical foundation for more principled approaches.

### [175] [Recovering Clinical Utility Under Differential Privacy: Empirical Validation of Adaptive Federated Aggregation on Heterogeneous Cardiovascular Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19403)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究仅在合成数据上验证了FedCVR的服务器端自适应优化对差分隐私噪声的去噪能力，缺乏真实临床数据的验证。本文旨在填补这一空白，在真实多中心心血管数据上评估框架的临床可行性。

Abstract: Validating federated learning frameworks on real clinical data is an essential step between proof-of-concept demonstrations in controlled synthetic environments and deployment in real multicenter healthcare settings. A prior architectural study by the same authors (Tertulino and Alencar, 2026) demonstrated, on a synthetic six-feature benchmark, that server-side adaptive optimization acts as a temporal denoiser for Differential Privacy noise, answering an open challenge identified in the original pipeline work (Tertulino, 2025). That study used synthetically generated data and explicitly identified real-world validation as a priority future direction. The present work addresses this gap by validating the FedCVR framework on five publicly available real cardiovascular datasets (Framingham, Cleveland, Hungarian, Switzerland, and Long Beach VA), harmonized to the 13-attribute UCI Heart Disease schema and configured as a heterogeneous federated scenario with leave-one-institution-out cross-validation. Results demonstrate that FedCVR preserves its adaptive advantage on real data, achieving an F1-Score of 79.2% and AUC of 0.96 under the operational privacy budget (noise multiplier = 0.8, privacy budget epsilon approximately 4.2), while statistically outperforming standard FedAvg on all evaluated metrics (paired t-tests, all p <= 0.003, significant under the Bonferroni-corrected threshold). ### [176] [Structured Latent Space Modeling over Multi-Scale Temporal Patches for Multivariate Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19404)
*Xingsheng Chen,Deyu Yi,Siu-Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: M2Patch是一种基于CNN的多变量时间序列预测架构，通过多尺度分块、深度可分离卷积和两种差异化约束（尺度内平滑性、尺度间对齐）来组织结构化潜在空间，在10个基准的40个预测设置中取得57个最优和34个次优结果，且保持线性计算复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间序列预测模型将学习到的表示为预测的瞬时副产品，未能充分利用跨多个时间尺度的结构模式的几何组织信息。

Method: 提出M2Patch架构：1）多尺度分块将输入分解为重叠的时间粒度；2）渐进膨胀深度可分离卷积提取尺度特定特征；3）每尺度可学习投影压缩为紧凑潜在表示；4）尺度内平滑性约束保证相邻分块的时间连续性；5）通过可学习的跨尺度映射实现尺度间对齐约束，恢复跨粒度交互。

Abstract: Multivariate time series encode structural patterns that unfold across multiple temporal scales, yet most forecasting backbones treat learned representations as transient byproducts of prediction, leaving the organizational geometry of these patterns underexploited. We introduce M2Patch, a CNN-based forecasting architecture that maps channel-independent multivariate observations into a structured latent space through two complementary differentiable constraints. Multi-scale patching decomposes the input into overlapping temporal granularities; depthwise separable convolutions with progressive dilation extract scale-specific features in linear time; and per-scale learned projections compress these features into a compact latent representation. The latent space is organized by an intra-scale smoothness constraint that enforces temporal continuity between adjacent patches, and an inter-scale alignment constraint, realized through learnable cross-scale mappings, that restores cross-granularity interaction within the channel-independent design, ensuring that all scales encode mutually consistent representations of the underlying dynamics. Experiments on ten real-world benchmarks show that M2Patch achieves 57 best and 34 second-best results across 40 forecasting settings, matching or exceeding representative baselines on most benchmarks while maintaining linear computational complexity and robustness to patch-level input corruption.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有进化策略微调LLM的结论存在明显矛盾：交叉熵奖励N=1即可，二进制奖励却需N≈30。作者试图解释这一差距的根本原因。

Method: 对比z-score优势归一化的影响；通过理论推导二进制准确率奖励下的零优势概率闭合公式，并在Qwen2.5-Instruct/GSM8K上以MAE 0.020验证。

Result: 禁用归一化后，二进制奖励ES在0.5B-7B模型上N=2即可在GSM8K和TREC上取得提升；归一化变体反而崩溃或退化。零优势概率公式与实验高度吻合，且能力较强模型下的N_avail很小。

Conclusion: 小种群在二进制ES中的失败是实现伪影而非内在限制，奖励粒度决定了种群需求的下界。

Abstract: Using Evolutionary Strategies (ES) for fine-tuning large language models is attractive because it is memory-efficient, parallel, and compatible with black-box or discrete rewards. Yet its population-size conclusions conflict sharply: fine-tuning with cross-entropy (CE) reward succeeds with $N=1$, while binary-reward training often needs $N \approx 30$. We show this gap is largely about reward design and normalization, not population size. In the capable-model regime we study, z-score advantage normalization can cause $N=2$ to fail. Disabling normalization lets binary-reward ES with $N=2$ improve on GSM8K and TREC across capable models spanning 0.5B-7B, where the normalized variant collapses or degrades. This small-$N$ risk is set by reward granularity: binary accuracy reward induces a zero-advantage probability $q$ that depends in closed form on base accuracy, batch size, and intra-pair correctness correlation; a zero-training probe on Qwen2.5-Instruct/GSM8K matches the formula with mean absolute error 0.020 across 12 configurations and finds the availability threshold $N_{\mathrm{avail}}$ to be small in this capable-model regime. The implication is not that $N=2$ is universally sufficient, but that small-population failure in capable-model binary ES can be an implementation artifact rather than an intrinsic population limit.

### [181] [Koopman Dreamer: Spectrally Constrained Latent Dynamics for Stable World-Model Imagination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19719)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Latent world models improve sample efficiency in continuous control by optimizing policies over imagined latent trajectories, but common neural transitions offer limited direct control over modal persistence and error accumulation in long rollouts. We propose Koopman Dreamer, a Dreamer-style world model with a spectrally constrained deterministic latent dynamics core. Its Koopman-inspired backbone uses two-dimensional rotation--scaling blocks with bounded radii to represent damping, rotation, and near-periodic modes. Linear and low-rank bilinear action terms capture global and state-dependent control effects, while stochastic-state modulation supplies local correction information. To reduce the mismatch between posterior-conditioned training and prior-only imagination, the model combines posterior-conditioned EMA teacher targets with one-step consistency, multi-step rollout, and open-loop observation-prediction objectives. We further derive a multi-step rollout-error bound that separates amplification by the spectral backbone and bilinear interaction from the additive effects of stochastic-state mismatch and modeling residuals, clarifying the trade-off between error attenuation and long-term information retention. Experimental results on proprioceptive continuous-control tasks from the DeepMind Control Suite and UAV-LiDAR autonomous navigation demonstrate that Koopman Dreamer improves the stability of long-horizon latent rollouts and achieves stronger closed-loop control performance on tasks that rely on high-quality multi-step imagination.

### [182] [Unlearning as Distribution Restoration: A Controlled Counterfactual Study, a Validated Selective Screen, and the Limits of Oracle-Free Certification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19442)

Motivation: 现有机器遗忘评估普遍采用与重训练oracle匹配的标准，但该标准是否真正衡量遗忘尚不明确。作者希望厘清现有评估方法的实际行为，并寻找更可靠的评估方案。

Method: 构建受控的非ce-fact测试平台，以匹配重训练模型为参考基准，在45个模型-种子组合（涵盖5个开放架构家族）上系统审计多种无oracle筛查和证书式标准。提出基于参考模型的重校准方法，并引入可辨识性定理分析遗忘阈值的理论可行性。

Result: 1）常用的一致性标准会评估保留已学知识的模型为"合格"（遗忘事实偏差-2.82 nats）；2）参考模型本身在41/45细胞中无法通过固定的保留阈值，在31/45中无法通过自身的往返测试，仅在1/45中完全通过认证；3）基于基线的保留筛查作为必要测试表现良好（45/45拒斥注入模型，44/45接受参考模型，35/45检测实体路由抑制）；4）基于参考操作点的损害相对重校准可在15/45细胞中认证子集，其选择落在重训练噪声范围内（0.80 nats），而常用标准偏离5.17 nats；5）固定幅度的logit抑制攻击可在12/45细胞中击败全部前向测试；6）可辨识性定理给出了可无oracle遗忘阈值的事实边界，TOFU被预测为边界情况。

Conclusion: 常用的与重训练oracle匹配的评估标准存在系统性缺陷，不能作为遗忘的可靠度量。基于参考模型的重校准可提供更有意义的评估，但任何前向测试都不构成充分性证书。机器遗忘评估需要在理论可辨识性边界内谨慎设计。

Abstract: Machine unlearning is commonly evaluated by matching a retrained oracle on trained probes. In a controlled nonce-fact testbed with a matched retraining reference, we find this criterion can favor methods that retain held-out knowledge: candidates it rates adequate score held-out forget facts $-2.82$ nats below the never-learned level (cluster CI $[-3.16,-2.48]$). We recast unlearning as restoration to the matched reference and audit oracle-free screens and certificate-style criteria across 45 model-seed cells spanning five open architecture families. The reference itself falsifies an absolute retain/round-trip certificate: the injected model, which retains the retain set by construction, fails the fixed retain threshold in 41/45 cells and its own round trip in 31/45, and the reference fully certifies in only 1/45. A base-anchored held-out screen remains strong as a selective necessary test: on a sealed challenge suite it rejects the injected model in 45/45 cells, accepts the reference in 44/45, and partially detects entity-routing suppression (35/45); it is a necessary test with measured sensitivity, not a sufficiency certificate. A damage-relative recalibration anchored to the reference's own operating point certifies a small subset in 15/45 cells; where it does not abstain, its picks lie within retraining noise (0.80 nats) on the axes it optimizes, while the common trained-probe criterion sits 5.17 nats away (a supporting comparison, not a head-to-head benchmark). A fixed-magnitude logit-suppression attack defeats the full forward battery in 12/45 cells, so forward-only certification is not sound; our method is an empirical selective test for methods-as-produced. An identifiability theorem delimits which facts admit an oracle-free forget threshold at all, with TOFU as the predicted boundary case.

</details>

*Aarushi Singh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个轻量级黑盒审计框架，用于检测工具增强型LLM代理在遭遇静默基础设施故障（如HTTP 200空响应、空负载等）时的行为。实验发现：代理面对静默故障时，56.6%的情况下会捏造结果（Fabrication），而安全拒绝行为（USR）在基线中仅0.25%，但当系统提示中加入安全语言后，USR激增15.6倍，表明安全提示会意外诱发模型编造政策理由来解释工具故障。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建轻量级黑盒审计框架，(1) 注入四种静默故障配置文件覆盖12个生产级别工具桩；(2) 将代理响应分为三类互斥行为：诚实投降（HSR）、捏造（FAR）、不忠安全拒绝（USR）；(3) 在温度为零、中性系统提示下评估2个前沿模型和2个开源模型；(4) 进行消融实验，在系统提示中加入标准安全语言。

Result: FAR占主导地位（56.6%）；USR在基线中几乎不存在（0.25%，396个有效轨迹中仅1例）；加入安全提示后USR增长15.6倍（至3.95%），Fisher精确检验p<0.001，95%置信区间2.2%-6.4%；敏感工具（fetch_medical_record, retrieve_contract, fetch_user_profile）占USR实例的大多数。

Conclusion: USR是一种潜在行为，当系统提示中的安全词汇激活模型在工具静默失败时寻找政策解释的倾向时被触发。提出负载-响应不对齐启发式方法用于生产环境检测，并讨论了安全部署场景下的治理启示。

Abstract: Evaluation frameworks for tool-augmented LLM agents focus overwhelmingly on capability metrics or explicit tool crashes, leaving silent infrastructure failures and HTTP 200 responses with empty, null, or malformed payloads largely unaudited. We introduce a lightweight black-box auditing framework that injects four silent failure profiles across 12 production-adjacent tool stubs and classifies agent responses into three mutually exclusive behavioral classes: Honest Surrender (HSR), Fabrication (FAR), and Unfaithful Safety Refusal (USR). Evaluating two frontier and two open-source models at temperature zero under a neutral system prompt, we find that FAR dominates (56.6% of valid responses): agents treat empty payloads as real data, silently returning fabricated results. USR, in which an agent invents a policy or privacy rationale to explain the failure, is nearly absent at baseline (0.25%, one instance across 396 valid trajectories). Our key finding emerges from an ablation where we augment the system prompt with standard safety language ("prioritize user privacy and data security"), which amplifies USR by 15.6x (from 0.25% to 3.95%; 95% CI on ablation rate: 2.2%-6.4%; Fisher's exact test, p < 0.001). USR is a latent behavior, activated when safety vocabulary in the system prompt primes the model to reach for policy rationales when tools silently fail. Sensitive tools (fetch_medical_record, retrieve_contract, fetch_user_profile) account for the majority of USR instances. We propose a payload-response misalignment heuristic for production-level detection and discuss governance implications for safety-forward deployments.

*Yunjie Chen,Xiaoxin Chen,Fang Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: REGEN不直接对多个教师模型进行蒸馏，而是回收利用教师专业RL训练过程中产生的回放记忆（replay memory，即免费副产品），结合离线RL算法来训练通用模型，从而完全解耦 rollout 采样与反向训练过程。

Result: 在数学推理、代码生成和指令遵循任务上，REGEN以显著更低的训练成本达到了与MOPD相当的准确率。

Abstract: Large-scale online reinforcement learning (RL) is the predominant means of eliciting advanced abilities including long-term reasoning and agentic tool use in large language models (LLMs). However, continuing to scale it across vast task domains of interest remains challenging in both computational infrastructure and cost, especially when considering RL as merely a one-off learning stage. Recently, a widely used technique for distilling knowledge across various domains and training stages, multi-teacher on-policy distillation (MOPD), helps to decouple the RL stage, saving costs, while maintaining generality across vast domains. Nonetheless, similar to online RL, MOPD requires coupled inference and backward passes, which continues to limit its scalability and computational efficiency. To address these challenges, we propose REGEN: Replay-recycling for Expert-to-Generalist Distillation with Offline RL. Instead of distilling from multiple teacher models, REGEN trains a generalist by simply recycling the replay memory -- the free by-product of the teachers' specialized RL training -- and employing offline RL algorithms. REGEN completely decouples the rollout sampling from the backward training process and thus greatly reduces the training cost. Across mathematical reasoning, code generation, and instruction following, REGEN matches the accuracy of MOPD at substantially lower cost. It potentially turns online RL into a data synthesis process instead of a one-off learning stage, and can potentially be extended to large-scale post-training without requiring heavy computational load.

### [187] [Generating Bearing Vibration Signals at User-Specified Fault Probabilities Using PR-GAN and Counterfactual Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19455)
*Seyed Mohammadreza Alavi,Ardeshir Shojaeinasab,Reza Jalayer,Masoud Jalayer,Behnam Bahrak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出并比较了两种生成轴承振动信号的方法（PR-GAN和Wachter-style CF），以产生具有目标故障概率（0.25/0.50/0.75）的边界样本。实验表明，CF方法能更可靠地达到目标概率（误差0.005-0.008，成功率1.000），而PR-GAN误差较大（0.046-0.059，成功率0.501-0.680）但运行时间更短。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴承振动数据集中大多数样本的故障概率接近0或1，而处于中间概率（灰色区域）的边界样本非常稀少。这些边界样本对于维护决策（如是否需要额外检查或采取保守响应）以及研究决策边界非常重要，因此需要生成这类稀缺样本。

Method: 使用异构集成分类器的平均输出作为固定、可梯度访问的概率预言机。提出两种方法：(1) 基于训练的PR-GAN方法，扩展WGAN-GP，通过残差生成器编辑真实信号并推动分类器输出向目标概率靠近；(2) 无需训练的Wachter-style CF方法，直接优化每个输入信号以在保持与源信号接近的同时达到目标概率。

Result: 在CWRU和Paderborn轴承数据集上，CF方法平均绝对概率误差为0.005-0.008，容忍度内成功率1.000；PR-GAN平均误差为0.046-0.059，成功率0.501-0.680。CF更可靠地控制概率且需要更小的平均L1变化，但PR-GAN在大多数设置下运行时间更低。

Conclusion: CF方法在目标概率控制精度和成功率上优于PR-GAN，而PR-GAN在计算效率上具有优势。两种方法均能有效生成轴承振动信号中的边界样本。

Abstract: In bearing vibration datasets, most samples receive predicted fault probabilities close to 0 or 1, while samples with intermediate (gray-zone) probabilities are rare. Such borderline samples are important because they reflect conditions in which maintenance decisions may require additional inspection or a conservative response and are useful for studying decision boundaries. To address this scarcity, this paper proposes and compares two approaches that generate vibration signals whose predicted fault probability matches a target probability of 0.25, 0.50, or 0.75. We use the average output of a heterogeneous ensemble classifier with different architectures and random initializations as a fixed, gradient-accessible probability oracle. The first, training-based approach, Probability-Regularized Generative Adversarial Network (PR-GAN), extends Wasserstein Generative Adversarial Network with Gradient Penalty (WGAN-GP) and edits a real signal through a residual generator while pushing the classifier output toward the target probability. The second is a training-free, per-sample Wachter-style counterfactual (CF) procedure that directly optimizes each input signal to reach the target probability while remaining close to the source signal. We evaluate both methods on the Case Western Reserve University (CWRU) and Paderborn bearing datasets using mean absolute target-probability error, time-domain total variation, and frequency-domain log power spectral density (log-PSD) differences. Across all settings, CF reaches the target with a mean absolute probability error of 0.005-0.008 and a within-tolerance success rate of 1.000 on retained samples, whereas PR-GAN's mean error is 0.046-0.059 with success rates between 0.501 and 0.680. CF therefore steers the probability more reliably and requires smaller average L1 changes, whereas PR-GAN has a lower reported runtime in most settings.

### [188] [MoA-Structured Decode Attention DNF Derivation, KV-Cache Accumulation, GQA/MQA, and OpenACC Kernel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19456)
*Lenore Mulin,Gaetan Hains*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文利用数组数学（MoA）为Transformer注意力机制推导了四种内存最优的推理构件，包括单查询解码DNF、C/OpenACC GPU内核、多步KV缓存以及分组/多查询注意力，所有实现均通过PyTorch验证。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于MoA的Denotational Normal Form (DNF)推导，通过ψ-归约消除K^T缓冲区，利用Operational Normal Form (ONF)设计步幅算术和合并内存访问，通过MoA拼接操作实现高效KV缓存，以及通过ψ-选择推导GQA/MQA。

Conclusion: MoA方法能够系统性地生成内存最优的注意力推理构件，兼顾理论最优性与实际硬件效率。

Abstract: We derive four memory-optimal inference artifacts for transformer attention using the Mathematics of Arrays (MoA), each following directly from the forward-pass Denotational Normal Form (DNF) of with the query-row index fixed to the current decode step. The artifacts are: (1)~a single-query decode DNF in which the $ψ$-reduction eliminates the $K^\top$ buffer algebraically, achieving $(d_k + nd_k+ nd_v+ d_v)\times4\,{B}$ Dynamic Random Access Memory (DRAM) traffic result numerically verified to $\|{err}\|_\leq2\times10^{-7}$; (2)~a C/OpenACC Graphics Processing Unit (GPU) kernel with Operational Normal Form (ONF) stride arithmetic and hardware-coalesced memory access, verified to $\|\mathrm{err}\|_\infty=0$ (exact IEEE-754 floating-point arithmetic); (3)~a multi-step KV-cache with $O(d_k+d_v)$ per-step append via MoA concatenation $\#$; and (4)~Grouped-Query Attention (GQA) and Multi-Query Attention (MQA) derived via $ψ$-selection, achieving a proven $\frac {h_q} { h_{kv} }$ reduction in KV traffic. All programs are verified against PyTorch scaled_dot_product_attention.

### [189] [Total Variation Distance Estimation in Autoregressive Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19510)
*Eric Price,Kevin Tian,Zhiyang Xun,Yusong Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在三种访问模型下（样本访问、logit访问、带噪logit访问）估计两个自回归分布之间总变差距离（TV distance）的查询复杂度，并提出了比现有工作更优的算法。实验在SGLang和vLLM上进行，验证了方法的实用性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代LLM部署中，即使使用相同的固定权重，不同的推理优化（如批处理、自定义内核、量化）也会导致引擎生成分布存在显著差异。现有TV距离估计方法查询复杂度高，且缺乏对不同访问模式的系统研究，因此需要更高效的估计方法。

Method: 针对三种访问模型分别设计算法：(1) 样本访问下，利用$\widetilde{O}(n^2 K/\varepsilon^2)$个查询，其中$K$为下一个token分布的最大支持数；(2) logit访问下，使用$O(n/\varepsilon^2)$个查询，并证明紧界；(3) 带噪logit访问下，当概率值有相对误差$\sigma$时，使用$\widetilde{O}((n+n^2\sigma^2)/\varepsilon^2)$个查询。

Result: 样本访问下查询复杂度从$\widetilde{O}(n^3 m/\varepsilon^5)$降至$\widetilde{O}(n^2 K/\varepsilon^2)$；logit访问下达到最优$O(n/\varepsilon^2)$；带噪logit访问下实现了样本访问与logit访问的平滑插值。实验表明TV距离在KL散度无穷大时仍可估计，且算法在实际部署中表现鲁棒。

Conclusion: 本文为LLM部署中分布差异的定量评估提供了高效的TV距离估计方法，理论和实验均证明了其优越性，代码已开源。

Abstract: Modern LLM deployments use a number of implementation choices and inference optimizations (e.g., batching, custom kernels, and quantization) on top of fixed weights, so two engines serving "the same model" can produce meaningfully different distributions. We study the problem of estimating the total variation (TV) distance between two length-$n$ autoregressive distributions to additive error $\varepsilon$, under three access models. (1) Under sample access, we use $\widetilde{O}(n^2 K/\varepsilon^2)$ queries, where $K$ is the maximum support of the next-token distribution. This improves upon the $\widetilde{O}(n^3 m/\varepsilon^5)$-query estimator of Meel et al. (2025), where $m \geq K$ is the total size of the token alphabet. (2) Under logit access, we use $O(n/\varepsilon^2)$ queries, and this is tight. (3) Under noisy logit access, we smoothly interpolate between the above two guarantees: if probability values are given to relative error $σ$, we use $\widetilde{O}((n+n^2σ^2)/\varepsilon^2)$ queries. We complement our theoretical results with an empirical evaluation of our algorithms, for example measuring the distance between SGLang and vLLM serving identical weights. Our experiments highlight the robustness and practicality of estimating the total variation distance, which remains estimable where the KL divergence is infinite. Our code is available at https://github.com/XunZhiyang/llm-tv-estimation.

</details>


### [190] [Do Sheaf Neural Networks Use Holonomy? A Measure--Intervene--Control Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19514)
*Ankit Grover,Rémi Bourgerie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出首个不依赖基底的训练三角形循环积测量方法，将旋转、茎空间面积和方向分离。在自定义高同质性GraphUniverse中，神经束传播（NSP）将三角形计数的SO(2)循环旋转从0.010提升至0.388弧度，而社区检测仅达0.029弧度。实验表明：替换学习到的SO(2)传输为单位映射会显著增加测试误差；但图谱岭回归预测器更准确，对角映射也有提升，固定度图虽旋转增加却未超越训练均值预测器。该测量-干预-对照研究分离了几何变化、连接敏感性与三角形特定计算的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 几何架构常通过旋转等内部机制来证明其合理性，但仅凭任务性能无法说明这些机制是否真正驱动了预测。本文旨在建立一套方法，能够直接测量训练后模型中几何结构的变化，并验证其与特定计算任务（如三角形计数）的因果关系。

Method: 以束神经网络（SNN）为测试平台，首次引入不依赖基底的训练三角形循环积测量方法，分离旋转、茎空间面积和方向。在高同质性GraphUniverse中应用神经束传播（NSP），通过测量-干预-对照（Measure-Intervene-Control）研究框架，比较不同任务（三角形计数与社区检测）下的旋转变化，并通过替换SO(2)传输为单位映射、使用图谱岭回归预测器等方式进行敏感性分析。

Result: NSP使三角形计数的SO(2)循环旋转从0.010增至0.388弧度，而社区检测仅0.029弧度。替换学习到的SO(2)传输为单位映射显著增加测试误差。图谱岭回归预测器更准确，对角映射也有提升，固定度图虽旋转增加但未超越训练均值预测器。

Conclusion: 该测量-干预-对照研究成功分离了几何变化、连接敏感性与三角形特定计算的证据，表明NSP在三角形计数任务中确实学习了与任务相关的旋转几何结构，而社区检测中则未出现类似现象。

Abstract: Geometric architectures are often justified by internal mechanisms such as rotations, yet task performance alone cannot show whether those mechanisms drive predictions. Using sheaf neural networks (SNNs) as a testbed, we introduce the first basis-independent measurement of trained triangle-loop products, separating rotation, stalk-space area, and orientation. In a custom high-homophily GraphUniverse regime, Neural Sheaf Propagation (NSP) increases the triangle-weighted mean two-dimensional SO(2) loop rotation from 0.010 to 0.388 radians for triangle counting, while the community-detection comparison ends at 0.029 radians. Across the training-set-size experiment, replacing all learned SO(2) transports with identities sharply increases test error, establishing post-training sensitivity to the complete learned connection. However, a graph-summary ridge predictor is more accurate, diagonal maps also improve, and fixed-degree graphs develop increasing rotation without outperforming the training-mean predictor. This measure-intervene-control study separates geometric change, connection sensitivity, and evidence for triangle-specific computation.

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) offers a promising approach to privacy-preserving clinical risk prediction, but its deployment remains limited by restricted data sharing, client heterogeneity, class imbalance, and the lack of realistic tabular electronic health record (EHR) benchmarks. Synthetic data generation may alleviate data scarcity, yet its integration with federated optimisation has received limited systematic study. Across federated settings with 5, 10, and 15 heterogeneous clients, SynPre-FL consistently improves robustness and scalability over baseline methods, especially under severe non-IID fragmentation. ### [193] [The C-index illusion: discrimination without calibration in published survival models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19526)
*Rafael da Silva,Danilo Alvares*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过复现三个不同领域的生存分析模型，验证了仅使用C-index评估模型会产生系统性误导：模型可能具有高判别力但校准严重失败（p=2.6e-136），风险估计存在偏差（最高达4个百分点），且概率估计随预测时间窗口退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: "Stop Chasing the C-index" 一文在合成数据上论证了仅用C-index评估生存模型会产生误导，但该论点在真实发表的非临床模型上尚未被验证。本文旨在填补这一实证空白。

Method: 复现三个已发表模型（硬盘故障、P2P信贷违约、用户流失），在三个不同领域上验证；使用锚定论文的合成实验验证评估工具；在Holm校正的族系错误率下检验五个预注册假设。

Result: 五个假设中三个被拒绝：(1) 模型判别力几乎完全复现（C=0.9595 vs 0.958），但校准严重失败(p=2.6e-136)；(2) 将提前还款视为非信息删失而非竞争风险时，违约风险估计偏高约2个百分点，高风险段达4个百分点；(3) 用户流失模型的概率估计随预测时间窗口退化，尽管全局判别力仍处于预注册C-index区间内。指标选择是否改变模型偏好排序的直接检验未拒绝。

Conclusion: 仅依赖C-index评估生存模型会导致对选定模型的过度自信而非选错模型；研究提供了可复用的预注册评估工具和完整代码。

Abstract: "Stop Chasing the C-index when Evaluating Survival Analysis Models" (ICML 2026, Spotlight) argued normatively, on synthetic data, that evaluating survival models by discrimination alone, i.e. the concordance index, produces systematically misleading model comparisons, because the metric ignores calibration and time-dependent accuracy. Whether this matters for real, published, non-clinical models has not been tested. We reproduce three published survival-ML models across three structurally distinct domains (hard-drive failure, peer-to-peer credit default, and user disengagement on digital platforms), validate our evaluation instrument against the anchor paper's own synthetic experiment, and test five pre-registered hypotheses under a Holm-corrected family-wise error rate. Three of five reject. A model that reproduces the published discrimination almost exactly (C = 0.9595 vs. 0.958 reported) fails a formal calibration test at p = 2.6e-136; a broad feature-ablation search finds no single attribute responsible for this discrimination, so the calibration failure is not an artifact of a trivial shortcut. A lender's estimated default risk is biased upward by roughly two percentage points, growing to nearly four points in the riskiest segment, when loan prepayment is treated as non-informative censoring rather than as a competing risk. A platform's churn model shows probability estimates that degrade with the prediction horizon even as its global discrimination stays within the pre-registered C-index band. A direct test of whether metric choice inverts which model is preferred does not reject, though with limited power given only two to three models per domain; the failure mode we document is better characterized as misplaced confidence in a chosen model than as choice of the wrong one. We release a reusable, pre-registered evaluation harness with full code and a single annotated notebook.

### [196] [End-to-End Differential Privacy in Training Deep Neural Network Classifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19580)
*Huaiyuan Rao,Calvin Hawkins,Alexander Benvenuti,Matthew Hale*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的差分隐私训练框架，在标签公开的条件下仅对训练输入进行隐私保护，通过在softmax输出层应用Dirichlet机制实现，并在多个数据集上取得了最优的准确率-隐私权衡结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有差分隐私机器学习方法通常同时对训练输入和标签进行隐私保护，但当标签本身是公开的或可以安全公开时，这种双重保护显得过于保守，导致不必要的精度损失。因此，有必要探索在标签公开条件下仅保护训练输入的新范式。

Method: 提出私有训练框架，保持标签公开，仅对训练输入进行隐私保护。针对具有softmax输出层的神经网络，将训练输入到softmax输出的映射视为到单位单纯形的映射。训练过程中对softmax输出应用Dirichlet机制（而非直接对梯度加噪）以实现差分隐私，并利用Rényi差分隐私理论对多次训练轮次中隐私损耗进行紧致界分析。

Result: 在CIFAR10、MNIST、MedMNIST、FashionMNIST、SVHN数据集上，所有评估的隐私预算下均达到新的最优准确率。在CIFAR10上，δ=10⁻⁵时，ε=4下准确率从78.37%提升至88.17%；ε=1时仍达到82.96%准确率，大幅超越现有方法。

Conclusion: 标签公开条件下的仅输入隐私保护范式显著优于传统双重保护方法，Dirichlet机制结合Rényi差分隐私分析能够有效平衡隐私保护强度与模型效用，为差分隐私机器学习提供了新的高效途径。

Abstract: Differentially private machine learning enables model training on sensitive data while ensuring that individual data is unlikely to be recoverable from the parameters of the resulting model. However, existing work often privatizes both training inputs and their labels, and these protections may be conservative when labels are public or can be safely made public. Therefore, in this work we propose a novel private training framework that instead privatizes training inputs while keeping labels public. We consider neural networks with softmax output layers, and thus the mapping from training inputs to the output of the softmax layer is a mapping onto the unit simplex. We randomize softmax outputs during training by applying the Dirichlet mechanism to enforce differential privacy for the training inputs, hence the ``end-to-end'' label. Because training data is reused across multiple training epochs, we use the notion of \Renyi differential privacy to formulate tight bounds on the strength of privacy provided by the Dirichlet mechanism across repeated uses. We show empirically that we attain new state-of-the-art accuracy when training from scratch on CIFAR10, MNIST, MedMNIST, FashionMNIST, and SVHN across all privacy budgets evaluated. Notably, when implementing $(ε, δ)$-differential privacy with $δ=10^{-5}$, we improve the prior state-of-the-art accuracy from $78.37\%$ to $88.17\%$ at $ε=4$ on CIFAR10, and our approach has $82.96\%$ accuracy even for $ε=1$, which significantly outperforms prior work.

</details>


### [197] [The Mechanism Matters: When Knowledge Graphs Help Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19616)
*Mohammed Sameer Syed*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过可控实验系统研究了知识图谱（KG）在强化学习（RL）中的注入效果，发现KG的结构性知识能提升样本效率和求解可靠性，但收益取决于任务相关知识的含量；更重要的是，注入机制的安全性差异显著——软性、最优性保持的注入能无害忽略错误知识，而硬性掩码在KG不完整或损坏时会导致灾难性失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献以单领域、正向结果的方法论文为主，缺乏对KG结构何时帮助、何时中性、何时损害RL智能体的系统性理解。

Method: 在MiniGrid环境中使用完全可控的合成KG，独立变化RL任务、注入机制（状态特征、动作掩码、基于势能的奖励塑造）和KG质量；并通过UMLS来源的败血症管理离线RL临床案例进行验证。

Result: 1) KG结构性能在组合稀疏奖励任务中提升样本效率和求解可靠性（70%→97%种子成功率），其收益来自结构而非泛化正则化（掩码p=0.0001，塑造p=0.006）；2) KG价值与任务相关知识含量成正比；3) 软性注入安全地忽略错误知识，硬性掩码在KG不完整或损坏时禁止必要动作，导致结果比无KG更差。

Conclusion: 为从业者提供了关于在RL中使用KG时如何信任以及多大程度上信任KG的实用指导。

Abstract: Knowledge graphs (KGs) are widely used to inject prior knowledge into reinforcement learning (RL), yet the literature is dominated by single-domain, positive-result method papers, so we lack a systematic account of when KG structure helps an agent, when it is neutral, and when it hurts. We conduct a controlled study that independently varies the RL task, the injection mechanism (state features, action masking, or potential-based reward shaping), and KG quality. Using a synthetic, fully controllable KG over MiniGrid environments, we report three findings. First, on compositional sparse-reward tasks structured KG guidance improves sample efficiency and solve reliability (70% to 97% of seeds), and a shuffle control that permutes the KG's edges while preserving their count collapses the benefit toward baseline (masking p=0.0001; shaping p=0.006), so the gain is structural rather than generic regularization. Second, KG value scales with the amount of task-relevant knowledge the graph contains. Third, and most consequential, safety depends on the mechanism: soft, optimality-preserving injection benefits from correct knowledge and harmlessly ignores incorrect knowledge, whereas hard masking is brittle, forbidding essential actions when the KG is incomplete or corrupted and making a wrong KG worse than none. A UMLS-derived clinical case study on sepsis management under offline RL is a careful null, underscoring that benefits require task structure the chosen mechanism can exploit. Our results give practitioners concrete guidance on how, and how much, to trust a KG when using it to guide RL.
